1b1(rgyud): be ti 'di la thams cad gsang ba 'jig rten gsum rgyal/ dpal mchog dang po/ ngan song sbyong chud/
1b2(rgyud): dpa' bo gcig tu bslab pa'i rgyud rnams bzhugs s+ho// /
2a1(rgyud): sarba ga h+ya na
2a2(rgyud): matan+ta ra dza/ bod skad du
2b1(rgyud): thams cad gsang ba zhes bya
2b2(rgyud): sa bya ba'i rgyud
2b3(rgyud): la po//
2b4(rgyud): dpal la phyag
3a1(rgyud): kye lnga yi bdag nyid can
3a2(rgyud): kyi lnga yi bdag nyid can/
3a3(rgyud): mi rnams lus la nges par mthong ba dag
3a4(rgyud): rang sems rab tu bsgom par gyur na ni/
3b1(rgyud): dngos der bsgoms pas nges par sangs rgyas 'gyur// rang
3b2(rgyud): shes gsang ba dam pa ni// sangs rgyas ye shes bla med de/
3b3(rgyud): gnyis med gnyis kyi tshul can te// sangs rgyas rtag par
3b4(rgyud): rab tu 'dud// gang yang bdag med rab tu 'dud// gang yang
4a1(rgyud): bdag med las byu shing // gnyis med
4a2(rgyud): ye shes las byung ba// sdug dang mi sdig rnams spangs pa/
4a3(rgyud): ci la'ang phyug ni mi 'tsha'o// ma skyes pa ni yang dag bskyed/
4a4(rgyud): skyes pa'i 'og tu rtag par ni// sangs rgyas skur ni bsgom pa
4b1(rgyud): de// rang gi ye shes mchog phyag 'tshal// garnal 'byor pa dang sems
4b2(rgyud): can kun// nyon mongs bag chags kyis sun 'byin// lus can rnams ni 'khor
4b3(rgyud): gyur par// sdug dang mi sdug rnam byed yin// sems gang de nyid sdug bsngal te/
4b4(rgyud): sems can rnams kyi lus 'byung ngo // sems de yis ni rgya nyid kyis// 'gro ba
4b5(rgyud): sdug bsngal gnod par 'gyur// rnam par snang mdzad rgyal ba mgon// sangs
5a1(rgyud): rgyas thams cad rtogs gyur pa// sangs rgyas 'khor ba
5a2(rgyud): sgrol ba po// sems can kun la phan pa'i phyir// thugs rje'i nyams dang yang
5a3(rgyud): dag ldan// rgyu'i de nyid mnyam sbyor bas// 'bras bu'i de nyid rnams kyang bsgom/
5a4(rgyud): 'bras bu'i de nyid yang dag bzhugs// rgyu'i de nyid mi 'dod do// gang du 'dod pa
5a5(rgyud): skyes gyur pa// de nyid 'khor ba'i bag chags yin// mkhas pa yi ni cho ga yis//
5b1(rgyud): bsgom pa ru ni yongs su brtags// gang zhig slar yang gcig 'gyur ba// rnal 'byor pa yi rnal 'byor byung //
5b2(rgyud): sangs rgyas rjes dran la dmigs nas// chos ni rjes su dmigs pa yis// tshogs gnyis kyi ni sbyor ba yis// rkang gnyis
5b3(rgyud): dam pa nyid du 'gyur// b+ha bar ling ga rab bzhag ste// sangs rgyas sku ni rnam par bsgom// sangs rgyas rjes dran rnal 'byor pa/
5b4(rgyud): sangs rgyasi sprin ni bsgom par bya// b+ha gar ling ga rab bzhag ste// rdo rje chos ni rnam par bsgom// chos ni rjes dran rnal 'byor pa/
5b5(rgyud): chos kyi sprin las char rab 'bebs// mtshan ma ling ga zhes bshad de// phyag rgya mtshan ma rnam pa bzhi// 'joms pas gsag ma
5b6(rgyud): zhes bshad de// nyon mongs 'joms pa'i dam pa yin// sems can kun gyi dngos kun gyi// rang sems chos ni bsdus pa yin//
6a1(rgyud): chos dag med pa'i sbyor ba yis// bas na rang nyid 'chi bar 'gyur// rang gi sems nyid rdzogs sangs
6a2(rgyud): rgyas// rtogs par bya ba'i sems nyid yin// rang gi sems nyid gsad dbya ba// sems nyid kho na gsad par bya// sbyor dang sbyor nyid yang
6a3(rgyud): dag 'brel// gang yang srid pa 'byung ma yin// gang tshe sangs rgyas de tshe ni// sbyor lnga sangs rgyas bdag ces bsgom// ting 'dzin ye
6a4(rgyud): shes las byung ba// sangs rgyas nyid phyir mdor bsdus pas// sangs rgyas rnal 'byor med par ni// rnal 'byor pa ni 'tshang mi rgya/
6a5(rgyud): phra mo'i sbyor ba ci bzhin mthong // stug po'i dngos poro de bzhin te// dngos dang dngos med khyad par ni// bsgom pa kun tu brtags pa yin//
6a6(rgyud): dngos po'i bsgom pa'i dngos ma yin// bsgom par bya ba bsgom pa yin// dngos po bsgoms par gyur pa yis// rang gi sems ni yongs su
6b1(rgyud): sbyong // sangs rgyas sangs rgyas yul ma yin// sems can yul du'ang mi 'gyur gyi// rang sems rtogs pas sangs rgyas te// sangs rgyas sangs rgyas
6b2(rgyud): rtogs par min// gnyis med sbyor ba 'di la yang // ting nge 'dzin gyi ye shes brtag/ rgyu'i de nyid ji ltar mthong // 'bras bu'i de nyid de nyid yin// rgyul
6b3(rgyud): de nyid cung zad med// 'bras bu'i de nyid de bzhin no// de nyid de ni de bzhin gshegs// de la rnal 'byor pa kun spyod// rgyu'i rgyu ni dngos por min// 'bras
6b4(rgyud): bu'i dngos por 'bras bu min// rgyu de 'bras bu'i dngos por rung // rang gi sems ni so sor snang // ye shes de ni rgyu dngos te// gsang de 'bras bu'i
6b5(rgyud): dngos po yin// gsang ba gnyis med sbyor ba yis// de'i dngos pos mchog yin no// de nyid de nyid rtogs gyur pa// gsang ste gsang ba'i rnal 'byor pa/
6b6(rgyud): gsang ba de rigs shes pa ste// mchog ni mchog gi rnal 'byor pa// sdug pa'i ngo bor gang bshad pa// mi sdug pa yang de'i dngos// sdug dang mi sdug gzugs
6b7(rgyud): gang yin// mi mthong de ni de bzhin gshegs// rnam shes tsam ni ming pa ru// rnal 'byor rnal 'byor 'byung mi 'gyur// ji ltar ye shes mcho ga dag pa/
7a1(rgyud): de ltar dag pa de bzhin gshegs// rnam par shes pa rnam pa bzhi// phyag rgya bzhi'i cho ga yis// gsang ba gnyis med
7a2(rgyud): sbyor ba yis// sku gsung thugs ni yang dag 'byung // thugs kyi phyag rgya chen po ste// dam tshig phyag rgya kun tu 'gro// chos kyi phyag rgya gsung gi ste// las
7a3(rgyud): kyi phyag rgya sku'i yin// rgya yis rgyas btab dngos po ni// gsang bdag gsang ba'i rnal 'byor pa'o// rang rig pa'i ngo bo yis// ting 'dzin ye shes
7a4(rgyud): brtags gang yin// lus ngag sems su rnams rtags pa'i// bya ba rgyud du rnam rtags pa// gsang ba rnam pa gsum du bshad// rdo rje las can sna tshogs
7a5(rgyud): bzhin// sangs rgyas lnga'i bdag nyid ni// gsang ba'i ye shes bla med yin// phyag rgya bzhi po gsang ba ste// rnal 'byor pa'i las grub byed// 'byung ba
7a6(rgyud): chen po bzhi po yang // phyag rgya bzhi zhes bshad pa yi// phyag rgya bzhi yi mnyam sbyor ba// lha mo bzhi dang yang dag ldan// sa ni spyan zhes bshad pa yin//
7a7(rgyud): chu ni ma ma ki zhes bshad// me dang rAng zhes grags pa ni// gos dkar mo dang sgrol ma yin// chu yi khams ni chu dkyil 'khor// dbang chen sa yi khams yin te/
7b1(rgyud): me ni me'i khams yin te// rlung ni rlung gi dkyil 'khor lo// dbang chen kha dog ser po ste/ gru bzhi pa ste rgyas pa yin// chu'i dkyil 'khor zlum po ste/
7b2(rgyud): dkar po mdog can zhi ba'i yin// me'i dkyil 'khor kha dog dmar// grwa gsum dbang gi las la'o// rlung gi dkyil 'khor gzhu'i dbyibs// nag pa
7b3(rgyud): gdug pa'i las rnams la// 'byung ba che'i bdag las grub// las kyi dngos grub yon tan gzhi// las kyi dngos grub dngos grub mchog/ 'khor los/
7b4(rgyud): bsgyur ba rnam pa bzhi// zhi ba la ni spyan gyi tshul// rgyas po pad ma'i rdo rje can// dbang la rnam par snang mdzad gnas// rdo rje khro bo mngon spyod pa'o// zhi ba
7b5(rgyud): dgengs kha bya ba yin// de bzhin rgyas pa snga dro la// bdag pa'i las rnams nyi ma'i gung la// dbang gi las ni mtshan phyed bya// zhi la dkar pos sbyar bar
7b6(rgyud): bya// ser po snang ba rgyas pa la// dbang gi las la dmar po ste// gdug pa nag po rab tu sbyar// ting 'dzin ye shes las byung ba// las kyi sgrub pa dam pa
7b7(rgyud): yin// bcom ldan dag pa bsgom bya ste// sangs rgyas 'gyur las mi g.yo 'gyur// b+ha ga'i dbus su gnas pa'i bdag/ rdo rje dbyings ni de bzhin gshegs/
8a1(rgyud): @lnga'i bdag gyur bdag nyid ni// bsgoms na g.yogs pa med par 'gyur// snying la gnas pa'i lha mo che// rnal 'byor
8a2(rgyud): ma ni rnal 'byor bskyed// sangs rgyas thams cad bskyed mdzad yum// rdo rje dbyings kyi dbang mor bshad// 'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug ste// 'di dag
8a3(rgyud): 'jig rten dug gsum yin// sangs rgyas bcom ldan dug mi mnga'// rdo rje dbyings ni de bzhin gshegs// chags dang sdang dang rmongs pa rnams// bsgom
8a4(rgyud): na khams gsum pa yi bdag/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'gyur te// sangs rgyas bden pas dag bcom mo// rang sems so sor rtogs pa yis//
8a5(rgyud): gti mug sems ni de bzhin gshegs// rmongs pa nyid ni 'jig rten gyur// sems can kun la lta bar bya// zhe sdang sems ni de bzhin gshegs// phra mo'i
8a6(rgyud): ye shes yang dag bskyed// sdang gyur rdo rje nyid du gyur// sems can thams cad gzhig par bya// 'dod chags sems ni de bzhin gshegs// byang chub
8a7(rgyud): sems ni yang dag bskyed// chags gyur bzang po nyid gyur pa// sangs rgyas thams cad chags par bya// byams pa'i sems ni de bzhin gshegs// nga rgyal/
8b1(rgyud): yang dag bskyed nas ni// mdza' bor gyur cing kun la gyur// sangs rgyas kun la 'khyud par bya// chags pa'i lta bas byams pa ste// thugs rje'i chos ni smra
8b2(rgyud): ba dang // kun la mi 'jigs sbyin pa dang // sangs rgyas thams cad mnyes bya'o// rnal 'byor sbyin las rab dga' ste// tshul khrims ldan pas dri med 'gyur//
8b3(rgyud): bzod pa las ni 'di byed pa// brtson pas 'od 'phro can dang ldan// bsam gtan las ni sbyangs dka' ba// shes rab kyi ni mngon gyur mthong // thabs chen
8b4(rgyud): las ni ring du song // stobs dang ldan pas mi g.yo 'gyur// smon lam gyi ni legs blo ldan// ye shes ldan la chos kyi sprin// rgyal ba de bzhin gshegs pa ni//
8b5(rgyud): rang rib bdag nyid bcu gcig gyur// pha rol phyin pa bcu rnams dang // stobs dang dbang ni rdzogs gyur cing // sa bcu la ni 'das gyur pa// mtshan ma brtan gyur
8b6(rgyud): de las ni// rdo rje'i chu ni rdzogs sangs rgyas// chos kyi bdud rtsi bcud len yin// sangs rgyas kun gyi mtha' yas pa// gzung dang 'dzin pa spangs pa yin/
8b7(rgyud): chos kyi bdud rtsi bcud len yin// rdo rje'i chu ni dag 'bung bas// rdo rje slong gyur rnal 'byor pa// gdod nas dag par de tshe gyur// gdod nas dag par gnas
9a1(rgyud): gyur pa// de nas byang chub sems su 'gyur// byang chub sems kyi bdag can gyur// byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs
9a2(rgyud): rnam par grol ba ngas kyi g.yogs// byang chub sems ni bla na med// yang dag bskyed gyur rnal 'byor pa// rdo rje sems dpa' snying la 'dag/ sems can
9a3(rgyud): khams ni mtha' yas pa'i// mar 'gyur dam tshig 'dzin byed dam// rdo rje dam tshig gis sbyang na// rtag tu dam tshig gnas par 'gyur// khams gsum las
9a4(rgyud): ni nyams dga' ba/ bud med ces bshad ji snyed pa// cho ga bzhin du kun sgrub cing // thugs kyi rdo rje rmad mi bya// rdo rje gsum gyi sku la gnas// dam tshig phyag rgya
9a5(rgyud): ji snyed pa// rdo rje dam tshig gsum gyis bya// gsung gi rdo rje smad mi bya// rdo rje sems las byung ba yi// phyag rgya kun ni bud med bzang // de rnams brtan pa'i rnal
9a6(rgyud): 'byor pa// phyag rgya thams cad dbang du gyur// 'jig rten khams ni thams cad du// bud med ces bya ci snyed pa// phyag rgya chen po'i sbyor ba yis// de dag kun la nye
9a7(rgyud): bar spyad// gsang ba mchog gi rnal 'byor pa// ting 'dzin ye shes dam pa yin// gal te dngos grub mchog 'dod na// nga rgyal ma yin hUM ma yin// rig pa ma yin
9b1(rgyud): sngags ma yin// lag pa phyag rgya'ang mi bca'o// mchod rten gyi ni las mi bya// glegs bam dag kyang gla ga mi bya// dkyil 'khor dag ni mi bya zhing // rdo rje mchog
9b2(rgyud): gsum phyag mi btsal// slob dpon smad par mi bya ste// bla ma sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam// khyed kyi srog chags bsad par bya// brdzun gyi tshig dang smra bar bya//
9b3(rgyud): khyed kyis ma byin blang bya zhing // gzhan gyi bud med brten par bya// sbyin bsreg yang na bsam gtan ni// lus ngag yid ni mi byed pa// gzhan min sems kyis bya ba
9b4(rgyud): ste// 'di ni bsod pa'i mchog yin no// sngags rnams thams cad rab tu 'grub// rnal 'byor kun kyang rnam kun tu// de bas 'bad pa thams cad kyis//
9b5(rgyud): sangs rgyas chos nyid bsgom par bya// ma 'dres chos ni bco brgyad po// sangs rgyas chos zhes bshad pa yin// de rnams rtag tu bsgom pa ni// sangs rgyas
9b6(rgyud): chos ni bsgrub byed yin// bsam gtan bzhi dang gzugs med bzhi// rtag tu thob par byas pa dang // 'gog pa'i snyoms 'jug de yis ni// sangs rgyas byang
9b7(rgyud): chub rab tu bsgrubs// byang chub mchog ni sum bcu bdun// chos su yang dag bshad pa gang // de rnams bsgom pas dag pa dang // byang chub sems
10a1(rgyud): dpa' 'gro pan yin// 'gro ba rnams la spros pa'i sems// brtan zhing snying po rab bsgoms pa// shes rab ye shes rang
10a2(rgyud): bzhin dag/ gsung gi sgra ni rnam par spangs// 'jam pa'i gsung gi bdag nyid gyur// rdo rje smra bar de bshad do// pha rol phyin pa kun gyi zhabs// chos rnams zam
10a3(rgyud): cad rtogs mdzad pa// sems can kun don sprul pa yi// rdo rje las zhes bya bar bshad// sangs rgyas rjes dran yang dag grub// theg pa dman pa rnams spangs
10a4(rgyud): zhing // byang chub sems la rab zhugs pa// rdo rje srung bar de bshad do// sdig pa thams cad zad byed cing // de bzhin nyon mongs rnams sreg la// nyon mongs
10a5(rgyud): zad pa nyer len pas// rdo rje gnod sbyin de bshad do// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje rnams// bcing pa ru ni yang dag gyur// de nyid de nyid ye shes te// rdo rje khu tshur zhes
10a6(rgyud): bshad do// dam tshig phyag rgya zhes bshad do// dam tshig phyag rgya thams cad ni// rdo rje bsdams las yang dag byung // rdo rje khu tshur gnyis gyur pa// las kyi phyag rgya
10a7(rgyud): zhes bshad do// sdig pa thams cad zad byed cing // de bzhin nyon mongs rnams spangs pa// nga rgyal med cing snang ba med// mtshan ma med cing zhen pa med// bdag
10b1(rgyud): med mnyam nyid ye shes ni// rdo rje sems dpa' zhes byar bshad// gsang ba'i mnyam par sbyor ba 'di// ye shes pha rol phyin dge ba// rnam pa bcu gnyis yang
10b2(rgyud): dang byung // rdo rje'i pha rol phyin pa'i 'od// byang chub sems ni rab bsgoms pa// pha rol sangs rgyas nyid son pa'i// pha rol phyin thob ye shes ni// rdo rje sems
10b3(rgyud): mar bshad pa yin// bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhi rnams ni// shes rab pha rol phyin rdo rje// chos bzhi cig tu gyur pa ni// rdo rje rin tshon mar bshad do// gsang ba'i ye
10b4(rgyud): shes rdo rje che// de nyid pha rol phyin dge ba// pha rol phyin pa che las byung // rdo rje ches mang shes rab bya// pha rol phyin pa'i dge ba ni// sbyor ba'i thabs su rab
10b5(rgyud): brtags pa// rdo rje las par shes par bya// gang phyir de ni reg pa dge/ sgeg mo sbyin pa'i pha rol phyin// tshul khrims pha rol phyin dge ba// brgyan pa'i yan lag
10b6(rgyud): yid 'ongs yin// bla ma bzod pa'i pha rol phyin// ched du brjod pa'i chos pa'o// gar ma brtson 'grus pha rol byin// myur du sangs rgyas nyid brten pa'o//
10b7(rgyud): bdug pa shes rab pha rol phyin// tshul khrims pha rol phyin dge ba// me tog bsam gtan pha rol phyin// 'dod pa'i 'dam gyis mgos pa// mar me smon lam
11a1(rgyud): pha rol phyin// phyogs kun snang bar byed pa yin// dri ni thabs kyi pha rol phyin// dri ni bur sel dge ba yis// sangs rgyas kun gyi/
11a2(rgyud): thabs chen po// dbye ba rnam pa bzhi yis gnas// thams cad 'dod pa'i thabs chen po// rdo rje lcags kyu zhes bshad do// byang chub spyad pa spyod byed pa// rdo rje/
11a3(rgyud): zhags pa zhes bshad do// theg pa 'di la brten 'gyur gang // rdo rje lcags sgrog zhes bshad do// chos rnams thams cad ma skyes shing // gdod nas zhi ba mkha'
11a4(rgyud): dang mnyam// de lta'i tshul 'dir rab 'jug pas// rdo rje dril bu zhes bshad do// tshogs gnyis kyi ni sbyor ba yis// sems can kun gyi don ston pa'i// sems ni
11a5(rgyud): rang bzhin gyi 'od gsal// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor yin par bshad// yang dag rdo rje rtogs pa ste// 'dzin pa'i stong nyid lcags kyu yin// phra rab 'bigs pas
11a6(rgyud): mda' zhes bya// dgyes pas legs so zhes bya ba// spras pa rin po che ru bshad// gzi brjid ces bya nyi ma'i// bsgrengs pas tog tu bshad pa ste// rnam par
11a7(rgyud): dbye bas bshad pa bshad// 'dod chags dag pa pad ma yin// nyon mongs dag spyod ral bri ste// dkyil 'khor sbyor bas 'khor lo yin// dag ni brjod pas/
11b1(rgyud): smra ba ra ba shad// kun nyid sna tshogs rdo rje yin// gnyi ga'i sbyor bas go cha yin// 'jigs pa'i sbyor bas che ba ste// phyag rgya'i sbyor nyid 'ching ba yin// dkyil
11b2(rgyud): 'khor du ni gang bshad pa// yid kyi dkyil 'khor dam pa yin// gzhal yas khang ni ye shes te// sems kyis brtsegs pa sgreng ba yin// phyi'i gru bzhi pa gang
11b3(rgyud): yin// tshad kyis mnyam pa nyid gyur pa// byams pa la sogs sems gang yin// thig bzhi zhes ni bshad pa yin// chos kyi rjes dran sbyor ba nyid// gang de rdo
11b4(rgyud): rje thig tu bshad// lta ba kun las rnam grol ba// ye shes thig tu bshad pa yin// tshul khrims thos kyi dam pa ni// gang gi brgyan du bshad pa yin// dad dbang
11b5(rgyud): la sogs sems gang yin// rab lnga ni yang dag byung // rnam par thar pa bzhi po ni// sgo rnams su ni yang dag bshad// yang dag spong ba bzhi po ni// rta babs/
11b6(rgyud): rnams dang ka bar byung // dran pa nyer bzhag bzhi po ni// khyams rnams bzhi po shes par bya// rdzu 'phrul rkang pa bzhi po na// de ni sgo khyud rnam bzhi yin// byang
11b7(rgyud): chub yan lag bdun pa ni// phreng ba me tog chun brgyan pa// 'phags lam yan lag brgyad pa ni// ka ba brgyad ces bya bar bshad// sgrib pa gnyis las rnam
12a1(rgyud): grol zhing // ting 'dzin ye shes yis brtags pa// lam gyi ye shes khyad par rnams// rnga yab ces ni yang dag bshad// nyon
12a2(rgyud): mongs thams cad nges gcod phyir// nyon mongs 'phrog pas dra ba ste// yang dag spyod cing spong ba nyid// sel ba'i spong bas la gnas pa// tshogs gnyis kyi
12a3(rgyud): ni sbyor ba nyid// nyon mongs pa yi phyed 'phrog pa// dra ba phyed ces bya bar bshad// rang bzhin 'od gsal gang yin te// byang chub sems ni bla med yin// sems
12a4(rgyud): ni don kun rab bskyed pa// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor yin par bshad// shes rab ye shes rang bzhin dag/ de lta bu'i ting 'dzin gyis// thar pa snang ba gzi brjid
12a5(rgyud): che// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor yin par bshad// mtshon rtsi lnga ni yang dag bshad// lta ba lnga yis sbyor ba yis// ye shes lnga yi nges sbyor nyid// sangs rgyas
12a6(rgyud): lnga zhes yang dag bshad// nam mkha' bzhin du bdag med pa'i// rnam shes ye shes dam pa yin// ye shes de yis rgyan bshad pa// chags pa'i sems
12a7(rgyud): zhes bya bar bshad// chags bral las ni byang chub 'byung // chags pa'i sems las gzhan yin no// de la chags dang chags bral ba// byang chub
12b1(rgyud): sems zhes yang dag bshad// 'jig rten chags dang bral bas 'dul// phyag rgya'i dngos grub chags las byung // de ni thabs kyi bsgom pa dag/ dngos grub
12b2(rgyud): thams cad ster ba yin// ji ltar 'jig rten 'dul 'gyur ba// de ltar rnal 'byor pa yis sprad// ji ltar 'dul bya dag gyur pa// zhen pa kun du mchod par 'gyur//
12b3(rgyud): mtshan nyid gang zhig yang dag bshad// mtshan nyid des ni mtshon par gyur// sku gsung thugs kyi phyag rgya'i// rgyas btab ye shes yin par bshad// phyag rgya
12b4(rgyud): bsgoms pas rnal 'byor pa// rtag tu phyag rgya'i bdag can 'gyur// rgyas btab dngos po shes nas ni// bsgoms nas phyag rgya btab par 'gyur/
12b5(rgyud): mtshan dang mtshan nyid 'brel pa ni// shes nas rnal 'byor yang dag spyod// ji ltar mtshan nyid yang dag grub// de bzhin dag pa myur du 'grub// g.yas pa'i cha
12b6(rgyud): ni mtshan ma ni// shes rab can ni rab du bstan// g.yon gyi mtshan ma ji ltar mthong // de'i thugs rje mtshon pa'o// phyag ni gnyis ka'i mnyam sbyor las// ting
12b7(rgyud): 'dzin gnyis su bshad pa yin// zhabs gnyis kyi ni mtshan ma yis// tshogs gnyis dag ni bstan pa yin// sor mo lnga'i mnyam sbyor bas// dkyil 'khor
13a1(rgyud): yis brgyan pa yin// sangs rgyas lnga'i mngon byang chub// rim pa bzhin du bsnan bya ste// gang zhig grung mo ston pa ni// nam mkha' las
13a2(rgyud): ni byung ba mtshon// gang zhig 'dzub mo ston pa ni// des ni dbang chen dkyil 'khor yin// srin lag du na yang dag bshad// chu'i dkyil 'khor zhes bshad do//
13a3(rgyud): gare zhig mthe bo ston pa ni// de yi mo ni mtshon pa yin// gang zhig mthe chung ston pa ni// rlung gi dkyil 'khor nyid du 'gyur// gang zhig lte ba ston pa ni// rdo rje dbyings/
13a4(rgyud): kyi dbang phyug bshad// gang zhig snying kha ston pa ni// rdo rje sems dpa' rjes su dpag/ gang zhig smin 'tshams ston pa ni// rdo rje rin chen ma zhes bya// gang zhig lkog
13a5(rgyud): ma ston pa ni// rdo rje chos mar shes par bya// gang zhig spyi bo ston pa ni// rdo rje las mar shes par bya// byang chub lnga mngon byang chub pa 'am// yang na ye shes lnga
13a6(rgyud): rnams sam// sangs rgyas lnga dang yang dag ldan// dkyil 'khor byang chub yin par bstan// sngon gyi sgra ni ji ltar bshad// phyi mar de ni yang dag bstan// gang du
13a7(rgyud): thog ma'i sgrar gyur pa// der ni rgyu'i sgra ru bstan// gang zhig mi'i sgrar 'gyur ba// 'dir ni 'bras bur yang dag bstan// sangs rgyas bcom ldan gnyis mi mnga'/
13b1(rgyud): rgyu dang 'bras bur ldan 'gyur min// gang zhig thog ma mtha' ma med// de phyir rtag pa zhes bshad do// rang sems rtogs pas sangs rgyas te// rtogs par bya ba 'ang
13b2(rgyud): sems nyid yin// sangs rgyas zhing zhes bshad pa dag/ byang chub sems su bshad par bya// rang bzhin dag pa'i sems can ni// kun du rig pa yang dag bshad//
13b3(rgyud): sems can rang bzhin dag pa yin// byang chub sems su shes par bya// dbang por gyur pa snying khar rde bas// brtan pa nyid du'ang rang nyid 'gyur// sgra 'dzin pa ni
13b4(rgyud): ral pa'i dbus// 'od dpag med pa mnyam bzhag yin// tsum pa nar gyi rjes bshad pa// de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje gsung // dbang po gnyis ni mnyam spor ba//
13b5(rgyud): rnam par snang mdzad ces bshad do// bu mo lo grangs bcu gnyis pa// skyes mchog thub pas gang gsungs pa// pha rol phyin pa bcu gnyis su// gsungs kyi gzhan
13b6(rgyud): du mi brtags go/ bu mo lo grangs bcu drag par// de bzhin gshegs pas gang gsungs pa// rdo rje sems sogs sems dpa' yi// bsgom pa'i don gyi sgra
13b7(rgyud): yin no// lha mo lo grangs nyi shu par// 'khor lo sbyar ba ji skad gsungs// mchod pa nyi shu'i bdag nyid can// nyi shu pa de rims bzhin no// rang gi chung ma rang rig las/
14a1(rgyud): byung ba'i rang rig yin par bshad// gzhan gyi chung mar gang bstan pa// gzhan sdug gzhan gyi rig pa yin// gci dang rdo rje zhes bshad pa/
14a2(rgyud): rdo rje ye shes bla med yin// gshang dang pad ma zhes bshad pa// chos kyi ye shes rnyog med yin// yongs su gsal bar rnam par shes// dkyil 'khor thugs kyi
14a3(rgyud): dam pa yin// sku gsung thugs kyi spyod pa yis// 'bad pa yis ni mchod byed pa// rang gi rdo rje pad mar ldan// dbang po gnyis las byung ba'o// rang gi khu ba
14a4(rgyud): thig le yis// rdo rje sems dpar mchod par bya// tshogs gnyis kyi ni sbyor ba yis// sangs rgyas thams cad gcig bsdus pa// gnyis med gnyis la rab/
14a5(rgyud): bstan pa// thugs rje nyams dang yang dag ldan// dbang po gnyis dang mnyam sbyor bas// rang gi khu ba mkhas pa yis// rnal 'byor chen po phyung nas ni//
14a6(rgyud): dkyil 'khor yang dag byin gyis brlab// dgod dam rab tu smra ba 'am// sangs rgyas rol mo'i gang byed pa// lha mo bzhi'i mnyam sbyor bar// rgyu dang mi rgyu rnams
14a7(rgyud): kyi rol// gsar zhing legs par sgril ba dang // tshad dang ldan zhing mdzes pa yis// shes rab can gyi thig gdab pa// sku gsung thugs kyi bsgoms pas so//
14b1(rgyud): zur bzhi pa la sgo bzhi pa// rta babs bzhis ni mdzes byas la// thig bzhi dang ni yang dag ldan// dar dang me tog 'phreng bas brgyan// grwa'i sa phyogs thams
14b2(rgyud): cad dang // sgo khyud kyi ni 'tshams rnams su// rdo rje rin chen spras pa ni// phyi yi dkyil 'khor thig gdab po// rdo rje thig gis yongs bskor cing // ka ba brgyad/
14b3(rgyud): kyis nye bar mdzes// ka ba gnas kyi nang gnas pa'i// dkyil 'khor brgyad par brtan pa dang // grwa'i dkyil 'khor dor bar ni// rdo rje lha me tshogs kyis mchod//
14b4(rgyud): 'khor lo lnga dang yang dag ldan// dkyil 'khor lnga yis rnam par brgyan// dra ba du phyed kyis spras shing // rnga yab kyis ni nyer spras pa// khru ni bcu gnyis bya ba 'am/
14b5(rgyud): khru bcu drug tu rab du brtags// yang na khru ni nyi shu tsam// nyi shu lnga dang ldan pa yi// khru ni nyi shu lnga pa yi// dkyil 'khor yang ni byin gyis brlab// sgo rnams kyi ni
14b6(rgyud): dbus mche// cha dgu ru ni rnam dbye ba// dkyil 'khor sgo ru bsams nas ni// sgo khyud der ni bya ba yin// sgo khyud dkyil 'khor rnam pa ni// snying po'i dkyil 'khor
14b7(rgyud): dang mnyam par// dgu cha ru ni rnam bsgos te// gru yi dkyil 'khor dor bar bya// tha mar byams dang ldan pa yi// dkyil 'khor lngas ni ldan pa dang // kha dog lnga da
15a1(rgyud): yang dag ldan// gru bzhi par ni brtag par bya// lta ba lnga po bgrod dka' che// kha dog lnga yi de bzhin gshegs// sangs rgyas lnga dang ma
15a2(rgyud): sbyor bas// sa ni mtshon gyis rab tu bsgyur// dkyil 'khor lnga pa dbus su ni// sangs rgyas lnga ni dgod par bya// kha dog lnga dang ting 'dzin gyis// 'dod pa'i yon
15a3(rgyud): tan lnga yis khyab// shel dang zla ba'i 'od 'dra zhing // sangs rgyas thams cad gcig bsdus pa// de bzhin gshegs pa rnam snang mdzad// dpa' yi lto ba de bzhin
15a4(rgyud): gshegs// in 'dra ni la'i 'od 'dra zhing // rdo rje thams cad gcig bsdus pa// mi skyed ye shes las byung ba// rdo rje'i lta ba de bzhin gshegs// 'dzam
15a5(rgyud): dbu'i gser gyi 'od 'dra zhing // sangs rgyas thams cad gcig bsdus pa// sems can kun gyi don du byung // 'bar ba'i lta ba de bzhin gshegs// dpa' bo/
15a6(rgyud): chen po pad ma 'dra// pad mar ge'i nor bu'i 'od// chos kyi ye shes las byung ba// chags pa'i lte ba de bzhin gshegs// ma rgad kyi ni 'od 'dra zhing /
15a7(rgyud): sangs rgyas thams cad gcig bsdus pa// sangs rgyas kun gcig las byung ba// byams pa'i lta ba de bzhin gshegs// dbus ma sa'i gzhi dag pa/
15b1(rgyud): nor bu chu shel mdog 'dra ba// shar phyogs nyid du sngon po che// lho ru ser po yang dag ldan// nub phyogs de ni dmar po ste// byang phyogs ljang khu yang dag ldan/
15b2(rgyud): kun tu khyams dang ldan pa la// sgor ni khyams dang bral ba'o// gang zhig du mar yang dag bshad// sangs rgyas ye shes bla med yin// gzhan dag don kun yang
15b3(rgyud): dag ldan// ting 'dzin ye shes dam pa yin// nam mkha'i dbyings kyis dbus gnas pas// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor dam pa bsam// sangs rgyas kun ni rnam
15b4(rgyud): bsgoms la// spyan ni dbus su bsam par bya// bzhin bzangs spyan ni yangs pa dang // nor bu chu shel mdog 'dra ba// mtshan rnams thams cad yongs su
15b5(rgyud): rdzogs// bud med sgyu ma'i mchog 'dzin pa// phyag tu 'khor lo bsgom bya ste// khams gsum pa ni dbang byed dang // dngos grub kun byed ye shes ni// 'khor
15b6(rgyud): lo yid bzhin nor bu'i mdog/ nam mkha' rdo rje dbus chud par// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor rnam par bsam// sangs rgyas sku ni rnam bsgoms pa// nam mkha'i
15b7(rgyud): rdo rje mchog bsgom mo// zhal mdzes spyan ni mang ba dang // ud dpal sngon po'i 'dab ma'i mdog/ mtshan rnams thams cad yang dag rdzogs// na mkha'
16a1(rgyud): sgyu ma'i mchog bsam mo// phyag tu ud dpal sngon po ste// khams gsum pas ni phyag byas pa// sangs rgyas byang chub byed pa'i
16a2(rgyud): mchog/ gsang ba'i dngos grub rdo rje can// nam mkha' rdo rje dbus chud par// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor dam pa bsam// sangs rgyas sku ni rnam bsgoms la// stong/
16a3(rgyud): pa'i de nyid las byung ba// rdo rje ye shes zhes byar bshad// chos bdag med las yang dag byung // gnyis med ye shes dam pa de// chos gnyis mchog gi ye shes
16a4(rgyud): ni// chos dbyings ye shes yang dag bshad// 'di ni chos dbyings ye shes te// de lta bu'i ting 'dzin skyes// rdo rje ye shes rang bzhin sems// rdo rje dbyings
16a5(rgyud): zhes bya bar bshad// sems kyis spros pa'i sbyor ba yis// phra mo'i ye shes sogs sbyor ba// de bzhin gshegs kun ye shes ni// rnam par snang mdzad zhes
16a6(rgyud): byar bshad// byams pa spros pa'i sbyor ba yis// spyod pa spyod par byed pa'i mchog/ zag med bstan par gyur pa yi// thugs ni mi bskyod pa zhes bshad//
16a7(rgyud): thugs rje spro ba'i tshul gyis ni// sems can phan 'dogs mdzad pa'o// thugs ni 'gro don yang dag ldan// rin chen 'byung ldan zhes bshad do// dga' bas
16b1(rgyud): spros pa'i sbyor ba yis// theg chen mchog ni dri ma med// thugs ni 'od gsal dag pa ni// 'od dpag med ces de bshad do// btang snyoms spros pa mdzad pa'i
16b2(rgyud): thugs// sems can thams cad rtogs mdzad pa// don yod bla med bya ba ni// don yod grub par de bshad do// byang chub rang bzhin ye shes mchog/ de 'dir
16b3(rgyud): rdo rje zhes bshad de// rdo rje ye shes las byung ba// rdo rje sems dpar de bshad do// sangs rgyas thams cad spyan 'dren pa// rdo rje lcags kyu zhes bshad do//
16b4(rgyud): rdo rje rigs rnams kun gyi rgyal// rdo rje rgyal por de bshad do// sangs rgyas thams cad tshogs byed pas// mnyes par byed pas zhes bshad do// bdud kyi sbyor
16b5(rgyud): ba chags pa che// rdo rje chags par de bshad do// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyes byed cing // legs so zhes pa rab stsol ba// byang chub sems dpa' dgo'
16b6(rgyud): byed pas// rdo rje legs par de bshad do// byang chub sems dpa'i sbyin pa gang // mkha' mnyam rdo rje las byung ba// don yod rin chen chen po de// rdo rje rin
16b7(rgyud): chen de bshad do// ma rig bral ba'i ye shes ni// tshogs rnams la ni nges par byung // thar par snang ba gzi brjid che// rdo rje nyi mar de bshad do// rnam pa kun
17a1(rgyud): gyi dngos ye shes// thar pa'i lam 'jug thob mdzad gang // chos kyi rgyal mtshan tog chen po// rdo rje dpal du de bshad do// rdo rje
17a2(rgyud): bzhad pa rnal 'byor che// sangs rgyas kun 'dzum rmad byung ba// 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' che// rdo rje bzhad par de bshad do// sangs rgyas kun gyi rnal
17a3(rgyud): 'byor che// sangs rgyas chos ni rtogs mdzad pas// de bzhin gshegs pa chos dag pa// rdo rje chos su de bshad do// shes rab rnon po theg pa che// nyon mongs
17a4(rgyud): thams cad nges gcod mdzad// shes bya'i sgrib pa bcod pa po// rdo rje rnon por de bshad do// sangs rgyas rol mo 'khor lo ni// chos kyi 'khor lo rab bskor
17a5(rgyud): ba// sems dpa' chen po theg pa che// rdo rje rgyu zhes de bshad do// rdo rje chos mar rnam par bsam// mdzes pa'i zhal dang spyan yangs pa// pad ma rag lta
17a6(rgyud): bu'i mdog/ sku mdog dmar po yang dag byung // chags pa'i pad ma 'dzin stug pa// mtshan rnams thams cad yang dag rdzogs// rgyan rnams kun gyis
17a7(rgyud): rnam par brgyan// rtag tu ud dpal dmar po ni// sangs rgyas thams cad rab bsgoms pa'o// chos kyi ye shes byed pa mchog/ gsang ba dam tshig rdo rje
17b1(rgyud): can// mkha' dbyings rdo rje dbus chud par// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor dam pa bsam// sangs rgyas gzugs ni rnam bsgoms la// sgrol ma mchog ni bsam par
17b2(rgyud): bya// zhal mdzes spyan ni yangs pa dang // sna tshogs rgyan gyis rnam par brgyan// kha dog ser po nyid bsam zhing // bud med sgyu ma'i dregs bde ba// rtag tu
17b3(rgyud): ud dpal dam pa ni// ser po snang ba bsam par bya// rdo rje nyid 'dzin las byung ba// sems can kun gyis phyag byas pa'o// oM ru ru s+phu ru dza la ti shA
17b4(rgyud): sid+d+hi lo tsa ni sarba aR+tha sad ni swA hA// au shang ka re shan ti ka re/ g+ha Ta Ta g+ha Ti ni g+ha g+ha ta ya g+ha Ta ti ni sA hA// oM ka tre bi ka tre ni ka tre ka ti ka te swA hA// oM ta re
17b5(rgyud): tud ta re tu re swA hA/ rig pa'i lha mo bzhi'i// skra ni lus kyi ngo bo yis// thugs ni sems kyi rnam pa nyid// gsung ni rnam dag rnam pa yis// mchod ni mchod
17b6(rgyud): pa'i bdag nyid 'gyur// sku gsung thugs ni gsang ba ni// mkhas pa yis ni bsrung bya ste// bsrungs nas mchog tu gsang ba ni// rtag par kun tu 'byung
17b7(rgyud): bar 'gyur// dngos po yongs su dag pa ni// med par kun tu rtag mi 'gyur// rnal 'byor pa ni rnal 'byor thob// tshogs med yang dag mi mthong ngo //
18a1(rgyud): de bas gsang ba'i ye shes 'byung // rnal 'byor kun tu 'byung bar 'gyur// shes rab pha rol phyin pa'i thabs// ting 'dzin ye
18a2(rgyud): shes brtags pa yin// chos rnams thams cad rnam dag pa// dag pa nyid du gyur pa ni// ji ltar lha yi nor bu ni// rang gi 'od kyi rtag tu snang // srid pa yongs
18a3(rgyud): su dag pa yang // rnal 'byor rnal 'byor thob byed yin// rdo rje dbyings ni gsang chen du// gang zhig dbang bskur mkhas pa la// thugs kyi gsang ba'i rnal
18a4(rgyud): 'byor mchog/ mkhas pas de la bshad par bya// thams cad gsang ba'i rgyud rdzogs s+ho// // rgya gar gyi mkhan po pad ma ka ra bar ma dang /
18a5(rgyud): zhu chen gyi lots+tsha ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos sgyur cing zhes te gtan la phab pa'o// dge legs 'phel//
18a6(rgyud): / rgya gar skad du// tre log kya bi dza ya ma ka la pa rA dza// bod skad du 'jig rten gsum las rnam par rgyal ba rtog
18a7(rgyud): pa'i rgyal po// dpal rdo rje sems dpa' la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa'i dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das ri rab kyi rtse mon rdo rje dang /
18b1(rgyud): nor bu rin po che'i khang pa brtsegs pa na/ byang chub sems dpa' bye ba phrag du ma dang / lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / mi 'am ci dang / 'byung po
18b2(rgyud): dang / sha za dang / brjed byed dang / mi rnams dang / bltar gyur pa dang / bltar mi rung ba du ma sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la mngon par dad pa rnams dang thabs
18b3(rgyud): cig tu bzhags te/ de nas bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje byang chub sems dpa' chen po nam mkha'i dkyil nas babs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs
18b4(rgyud): gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das la lan gsum bskor ba byas te 'di skad ces gsol to// yang bcom ldan 'das bdag gis lha
18b5(rgyud): chen po la sogs pa sems can ma rungs pa de dag dam tshig 'dzin du stsal ba na/ bcom ldan 'das de'i slad du bka' stsal du gsol// de nas phyag na rdo rje
18b6(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i tshig bcom ldan 'das chos kyi rgyal po de bzhin gshegs pas gnang nas phyag na rdo rje la 'di skad ces gsungs
18b7(rgyud): so// gnod sbyin khyod shin tu khengs pa/ shin tu khro ba/ shin tu 'thur ba ste/ ji ltar khyod kyis sems can rnams kyi don gyi phyir 'di lta bu'i sngags kyi tshig
19a1(rgyud): spras/ de nas bcom ldan 'das la phyag na rdo rje byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos 'di skad ces gsol to// ci'i phyir na
19a2(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das sems can ma rungs pa 'dul bar byed do// gang gi phyir zhe na/ bdag gis 'dod pa'i bde ba can rnams dbang du bgyi ba la sogs pas btul
19a3(rgyud): nas bla na med pa'i bde ba la bkod par 'tshal lo// sems can ma rungs pa rnams bsal ba la sogs pas sbyangs te zhi ba la bkod par bya'o// de nas bcom
19a4(rgyud): ldan 'das kyi phyag na rdo rje byang chub sems dpa' la legs so zhes bya ba byin te/ phyag na rdo rje legs so legs so// 'jig rten thams cad kyi don gyi phyir dang /
19a5(rgyud): phan pa'i phyir dang / bde ba'i phyir snying po 'di smros shig/ de nas phyag na rdo rje byang chub sems dpa' lha thams cad nas/ mi rnams thams cad kyi bad du sangs
19a6(rgyud): rgyas kyi bstan pa la mngon par dad pa de rnams la bka' stsal pa/ grogs po dag sangs rgyas la skyabs su dengs shig/ nga'i bka' rjes su skyongs shig/ de nas
19a7(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs gnyis la phyag na rdo rjes phyag 'tshal nas/ 'jig rten gsum las rnam par rgyal ba'i snying po 'di gsungs so// oM suM b+ha ni suM b+ha ni
19b1(rgyud): hUM/ grih+Na gri hA hUM/ b+hI pa ya grI pa ya hUM/ a na ya ho b+ha ga ba na bid+ya ra dza hU~M phaT/ de nas 'di gsungs pa tsam gyis 'jig rten gsum po thams cad g.yos/
19b2(rgyud): g.yos rab tu g.yos cig tu g.yos so// 'gul rab tu 'gul/ kun tu 'gul to// 'phar rab du 'phar/ kun tu rab du 'bar ro// de nas lha thams cad
19b3(rgyud): la sogs pa sems can thams cad 'dar yid yid nas bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der lhag nas/ kho ra khor yug dang / kho ra khor yug chen po'i ri la sogs pa
19b4(rgyud): tshun chad kyi gling bzhi'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad sems can gyis gang ngo // de nas bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams tshegs
19b5(rgyud): pa'i dkyil 'khor thams cad la gzigs nas 'di skad ces gsungs so// grogs po rnams sangs rgyas la brtson pa la skyabs su 'gro bar khas long shig
19b6(rgyud): nga'i bka' rjes su skyongs shig/ de nas 'dus pa'i 'khor chen po thams cad bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rjes skrags te 'dor yid yod nas bcom ldan 'das de
19b7(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa la skyabs su dong ngo // de nas bcom ldan 'das la lha chen po'i lha dang / mthu bo che dang / tshangs pa rnams kyis 'di skad ces gsol to//
20a1(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das 'di lta bu'i sems can 'di ltar rdzu 'phrul che ba/ 'di ltar byin che ba zhing bdag cag la chos 'di su lags//
20a2(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis bstan pa'i phyir tshigs su bcad pa 'di grangs te gsungs so// sems can kun la phan pa'i phyir// sangs rgyas kun gyis byin
20a3(rgyud): gyis brlabs// kun tu bzang po kun gyi bdag sangs rgyas thams cad nyid skyes 'di// phyag na rdo rje gnod sbyin che// ma rungs chos la dbang ba ste// gang gi/
20a4(rgyud): ming brjod pa yis ni// sangs rgyas pa yang thob par 'gyur// de nas phyag na rdo rje byang chub sems dpa' chen po la yang gsungs pa// kye kye lha dag sangs
20a5(rgyud): rgyas la skyabs su deng la nga'i bka' bzhin du yang gyis shig/ rdo rje 'bar ba gcig tu 'bar bar 'gyur ba 'dis// khyed thams cad rten bsregs par gyur ta
20a6(rgyud): re/ de nas lha chen po la sogs pa thams cad kyis 'di skad ces smras so// khyed ni gnod sbyin dang ni lta bas na ngad ni gnod sbyin gyi bka' rjes su sbyong bar mi nus so//
20a7(rgyud): de nas phyag na rdo rje de thos nas khros te bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' bstsal pa/ bdag ma rungs
20b1(rgyud): pa thams cad 'dul bar dbang bskur bar bskos te/ de bas na lags te bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' bstsal to// lha chen po 'di 'dul bar 'tshal lo// de nas
20b2(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das kyis lha chen po la 'di skad ces gsungs so// sems can chen po khas long shig/ 'dis khyod gsad ta re/ de nas bcom ldan 'das la lha
20b3(rgyud): chen po la sogs pa 'jig rten gsum thams cad kyi dbang po rnams kyis 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das gnod sbyin ma rungs pa 'di'i bka' bzhin du
20b4(rgyud): byed pa bdag cag mi nus lags so// de nas lha chen pos bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs gnyis la phyag 'tshal nas bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje la 'di skad ces
20b5(rgyud): smras so// kye gnod sbyin de ni thams cad kyi dbang po byed pa po 'jom pa po// skye dgu'i bdag po tshangs pa'o// rtogs 'dod do// dbang phyug chen po'o// de nas
20b6(rgyud): phyag na rdo rje byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po khros nas 'di skad gsungs so// khyod ni lus sbrul po mi za ba ma rungs pa drag shul gyi las byed pas na
20b7(rgyud): gtum po ste/ sha za ba'i lus srel ba na ji ltar tshangs pa dang / rtogs 'dod dang / dbang phyug chen po dang / tshangs pa zhes bya ba ni mi 'gyur ba'o// rtogs 'dod
21a1(rgyud): ces bya ba ni thar pa'o// dbang phyug chen po zhes bya ba ni 'dod pa'i khams kyi dbang po ste/ sems can thams cad kyi dbang po ste de ni yin
21a2(rgyud): pas btul nus so// de nas dbang phyug chen po lha chen po khros nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs gnyis la phyag 'tshal nas 'jigs su rung ba chen po'i gzugs
21a3(rgyud): khros pa chen po'i gad mos bkod nas 'jigs pa chen por byed pa/ 'bar ba chen po gtong ba/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad mtha' med pa/ gzugs sna tshog
21a4(rgyud): su byas pa/ 'bar ba chen po grub pa/ mi mtshungs pa/ rdo rje dang / mdung rtse gsum pa dang / 'khor lo dang / shag tig dang / be con dang / mi mtshungs pa'i mtshon
21a5(rgyud): cha 'debs shing gtong ba/ mi rnams kyi tshogs dang / 'byung po'i tshogs dang bcas pas kun tu bstan to// bdud dang bgegs byed pa dang mu med pa'i gzugs sna
21a6(rgyud): cho gas su sprul pa/ khros pa rab tu mi bzod pa/ ma rungs pa'i tshogs chen po dang lhan cig tu rab du 'thab cing shin tu 'gyed pa/ gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams
21a7(rgyud): mtshon pa'i mun nag byas/ 'bar ba chen po'i phung bas glongs te rab du snang bar byas/ de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'chang chen po cung zad mche ba'i thog ma cigs pa/
21b1(rgyud): srin 'tshams kyi khro gnyer gyi brlags bskyod pa mig g.yon pa cher bskrad de/ rdo rje'i lta bas khro ba dang bcas pas zab mo'i tshig gis snying po mchog 'jig rten gsum
21b2(rgyud): las rgyal ba'i dpal zhes bya ba 'di gsungs so// hUM de nas hUM zhes bya ba des stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kun sgra des gang nas/ g.yos rab tu
21b3(rgyud): g.yos/ kun tu rab du g.yos so// khro la rab tu khrol/ kun tu rab tu khrol lo// de nas dbang phyug chen po la sogs pa lha'i tshogs thams cad bcom ldan 'das
21b4(rgyud): skyabs du gsol/ bde bar gshegs pa smra ba da gsol zhes brjod nas/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis phyag na rdo rje la 'di skad ces gsungs so// gang 'di lta bu'i
21b5(rgyud): sngags kyi tshig smra ba ni khyod rab tu mi bsgrub po// de nas phyag na rdo rjes bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs gnyis la phyag 'tshal nas yang 'jig rten gsum las rnam par
21b6(rgyud): rgyal ba 'di gsungs so// oM suM b+ha ni su~M b+ha ni hUM/ gr-ih+Na gr-ih+Na hUM/ grih+NA pa ya grih+NA pa ya hUM/ a na ya ho b+ha ga ban bid+ya ra dza hUM phaT/ de nas 'di gsungs pa tsam
21b7(rgyud): gyis lha chen po la sogs pa lha'i bdag po thams cad 'khor dang bcas par bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje gan ba der mgo rkang bzlog te// ri rab ri'i rtse mor dkyil
22a1(rgyud): 'khor chen por btsud nas brlabs par bya ste/ bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje'i zhabs g.yon pas mnan to// de nas bcom ldan 'das
22a2(rgyud): phyag na rdo rje byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po la legs so zhes bya ba byin te/ phyag na rdo rje legs so legs so khyod kyis 'di 'dra ba'i sems can 'dul
22a3(rgyud): bar byed pa legs so legs so// de bas na thul la dbugs phyung shig/ de nas bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos de
22a4(rgyud): dag gi don gyi phyir rdo rje bcings pa 'di gsungs so// hUM badz+re tI to me pa rak+Sha sarba na swA hA/ de nas phyag na rdo rje 'di gsungs pa tsam gyis lha chen po la sogs pa
22a5(rgyud): de dag thams cad dran pa rnyed do// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de dag la 'di skad gsungs so// de bas grogs po dag sems can chen po 'di'i bka' bzhin/
22a6(rgyud): byed par kha sa long shig/ de nas bcom ldan 'das la de dag thams cad mgrin cig tu bdag cag mchod kyis 'tshal lo zhes gsol to// de nas phyag na rdo rje byang
22a7(rgyud): chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos rang gi snying po 'di gsungs so// oM ta ki hU~M/ de nas 'di brjod pa tsam gyis lha la sogs pa thams cad dbang du byas te/
22b1(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje la phyag byas mchi ma blags te/ nga ro ston nas skyabs su dong ste bcom ldan 'das skyab du gsol/ bdag cag khyed kyi bka' nyan dza
22b2(rgyud): ltar bgyi ba bka' stsal du gsol zhes so// de nas phyag na rdo rje byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos de rnams la gsungs pa/ grogs po dag byang
22b3(rgyud): chub kyi sems dang / ston pa bzung bar khas long shig/ bcom ldan 'das bdag cag gis sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bsnyen bkur bgyid cing
22b4(rgyud): byang chub tu yang sems bskyed par 'tshal lo// de nas phyin na rdo rje byang chub sems dpa' de rnams ji lta ba bzhin du dkyil 'khor du btsud nas sdom pa 'dzin du
22b5(rgyud): bcug ste/ byang chub sems ni bstan byas la// sems can thams cad bde ba rtsa la// phyag na rdo rje bdag chen dang // 'dod pa smad par mi bya'o// 'di ni gsad
22b6(rgyud): ba yin no// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de dag sdom pa 'dzin du bcug de/ dam tshig sbyin pa ni/ oM badz+ra sa ma ya a bi Shin tsam ba ra ga ya sarba ka man ts+tsha paT
22b7(rgyud): de nas de dag gis smras pa/ 'di ni bdud kyis smras pa na bdag cag nyan to// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pas de dag la khyod cag gis 'di la/
23a1(rgyud): ma rnyas shig ces gsungs pa dang / de dag gis gsungs pa dang / ji ltar 'dod chags dang bral ba ni sangs rgyas kyi byang chub bo
23a2(rgyud): zhes bcom ldan 'das nyid kyis bka' stsal to// bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa/ kye grogs po dag pa ni ji ltar 'dul byed bzhin du byed pa ste/
23a3(rgyud): 'di nyid kyis 'jig rten gyi khams 'di sun 'byin te/ ji ltar bde ba la mi chags pa dang / sdug bsngal la 'dod chags pa can lta bu 'jig rten 'dadul bar
23a4(rgyud): 'gyur ba'i chos sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams brtsal bar mdzad de/ de dag spyad pa'i phyir 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kun tu bzong po
23a5(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' ci nas 'dod chags dang bral ma byed cig ces bka' stsal to// de nas phyag na rdo rjes yang gsungs pa/ oM badz+ra sa ma ya a bi Shin
23a6(rgyud): tsam bai ra ga ya sa ma b+ha ga ma hUM phaT/ de nas de dag gis ji ltar bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' de de bzhin no zhes gsol to// de nas yang phyag na rdo rje lag
23a7(rgyud): tu rdo rje byin te rdo rje dbang bskur ba 'di byin no// oM badz+ra a b+hi Shin tsa sarba ta thA ga ta badz+ra d+ha rad de badz+ra ba ni hi hA ha ha ha/ de nas rdo rje ming gis dbang bskur ba/
23b1(rgyud): byin pa ni 'di lta ste/ dbang phyug chen po ni rdo rje rig sngags mchog/ dbu ma chen po rdo rje sgyu ma'o// tshangs pa ni rdo rje mi smra ba'o// sgra gzhon na ni rdo rje dril bu'o//
23b2(rgyud): dbang po ni rdo rje 'thab cha ste/ de la sogs te 'jig rten gyi dbang po thams cad rig pa'i blon por dbang bskur ro// de nas bar snang la rgyu ba rnams rdo rje ming
23b3(rgyud): gis dbang bskur byin pa ni 'di lta ste/ bdud ci 'khyil pa ni rdo rje 'khyil pa'o// zla ba ni rdo rje 'od do// be tsen rtse mo ni rdo rje be con no// skye blang ni rdo rje skye blang ngo //
23b4(rgyud): de rnams ni rdo rje khro bor dbang bskur ro// de nas nam mkha' la rgyu ba'i lha rnams ming gis dbang bskar ba byin pa ni 'di lta ste/ chang gis myos pa ni rdo rjes zin
23b5(rgyud): pa'o// 'chang byed ni rdo rje phreng ba'o// rgyal ba ni rdo rje dbang ngo // rgyal ba skyes pa ni rdo rje ming gis dbang rnam par rgyal ba ste/ de dag la sogs pa ni tshogs kyi
23b6(rgyud): bdag por dbang bskur ro// de nas sa steng pa rnams rdo rje ming gis dbang bskur ba byin pa ni 'di lta ste/ mdzad skyong ni rdo rje dang shing ngo // rlung ni rdo rje rlung ngo // me ni
23b7(rgyud): rdo rje me'o// ku be re ni rdo rje 'jigs pa ste/ de la sogs pa'i pho nyar dbang bskur ro// de nas sa'i 'og na gnas pa'i lha'i dbang po rnams yan chad rdo rje ming
24a1(rgyud): gis dbang bskur ba byin pa ni 'di lta ste/ phag ni rdo rje kyo ba'o// gshin rje nag pa'o// sa'i rba ni rdo rje rnam 'dren no// ba ru na ni
24a2(rgyud): rdo rje rlung ste/ de la sogs pa ni rdo rje bran du dbang bskur ro// de nas 'jig rten gsum gyi bdag po rnams kyis lha mo thams cad kyi lag tu rdo rje sbyin te rdo rje ming gis
24a3(rgyud): dbang bskur nas rdo rje ming gis dbang bskur ba byin pa ni 'di lta ste/ nyon mongs pa ni rdo rje khro bo'i me'o// nor can ni rdo rje gsung ma'o// tshangs mi ni rdo rje zhi ba'o//
24a4(rgyud): dug me ni rdo rje gzhon nu ma'o// dbang me ni rdo rje khu tshur ro// de la sogs pa ni rig sngags kyi blon me chen mor dbang bskur ro// de nas bar snang la rgyu ba'i ma rnams
24a5(rgyud): dbang bskur ba byin pa ni 'di lta ste/ bdud rtsi ma ni rdo rje ma'o// 'khrungs ma ni rdo rje sdug ma'o// be con 'chang ba ni rdo rje bo con ma'o// skye 'phrog ni rdo rje bskyed bcings
24a6(rgyud): te de la sogs pa ni rdo rje khro mor dbang bskur ro// de nas nam mkha' la rgyu ba'i me me rnams dbang bskur bar byin ni 'di lta ste/ bsod mo ni rdo rje bsod mo'o//
24a7(rgyud): zab mo ni rdo rje zab mo'o// gos ni rdo rje bge ba bya'o// dga' ba mo ni rdo rje dga' ba mo'o// de la sogs pa ni rdo rje tshogs ma mor dbang bskur ro// de nas sa la
24b1(rgyud): rgyu ba'i ma rnams dbang bskur ba byin pa ni 'di lta ste/ zhib mo ni rdo rje pho nya mo'o// rlung ma ni rdo rje 'gog mthong ngo // me ni rdo rje 'bar ma'o// ku be ra ni rdo rje thag zug
24b2(rgyud): ma ste/ de las sogs pa ni rdo rje pho nya mor dbang bskur ro// de nas sa 'og na gnas pa'i ma mo thams cad dbang bskur ba byin pa ni 'di lta ste/ phag mo ni rdo rje gdong //
24b3(rgyud): mgo lcags ma ni rdo rje nag po'o// sna tshad ma ni rdo rje myags ma'o// klu mo ni rdo rje chu srin ma ste/ de la sogs pa ni rdo rje bran mor dbang bskur ro// de nas phyag na rdo rje
24b4(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' chen po sa bcud de dag thams cad sangs rgyas kyi ye shes bskyed nas rdo rje dam tshig byin pa/ oM ba li bstod/ ba li ta badz+ra a kar sha ya/
24b5(rgyud): hUM dza/ lha rnams 'gugs pa'o// oM badz+ra a bri pi ta ya sa ma ya hUM/ bar snang la rgyu ba rnams kyi'o// oM badz+ra ma la gra ba/ phreng ba 'chang ba rnams kyi'o//
24b6(rgyud): oM badz+ra ban ta tsi/ sa la rgyu ba rnams kyi'o// oM badz+ra swa sta la badz+ra hUM phaT/ 'og na gnas pa rnams kyi'o// oM badz+ra he ru ka badz+ra sa ma ya sarba dusta sa ma ya
24b7(rgyud): mud tra ka pra badz+ra ka hU~M phaT/ ma rnams thams cad kyi'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs gnyis la phyag na rdo rje phyag 'tshal nas 'di skad ces gsol to//

25b1(rgyud): de nas phyag na rdo rje byang chub sems dpa' chen po bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la yid rangs te tshigs su bcad pa 'di smras pa// sems can kun la phan
25b2(rgyud): pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kun gyis byin brlabs te// grub pa thams cad byed pa'i mchog/ dkyil 'khor chen po bshad par bya'o// de nas yang dag bshad pa

26b1(rgyud): brgya rnams so// gnan dal dang ni nad dag dang // mkha' sgom dang gdon drag rnams// bzhag gam yang na bri bar bya// chos min can ni gzhig phyir ro// de'i phyi rol

26b4(rgyud): me tog bzhag nas snying po 'di brjod la zhugs shig/ oM badz+ra pra ti tsha ma ma ha ha ha ha hi/ de nas pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs nas du ru ki'i bdag pa

26b6(rgyud): nyi shu rtsa gcig bzlas nas/ de nas tshan ma 'byung ba ni ba spu g.yo ba la sogs po dang / sa g.yo ba 'am/ dri zhim po 'am/ 'od zer mthong ba de nas phyag na rdo rje'i sku

27a1(rgyud): slab pa'i sdom pa 'dzin pa so sor gnas par byas nas byang chub kyi sems bskyed cig/ de nas gdong ras kyi g.yogs/ mgo gtsug

27a5(rgyud): dkyil 'khor 'byung ste/ rdo rje'i phreng ba mnyam ldan pas/ rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor brtag par bya'o// 'jug par bya ba de bzhin te// las kyang de dang 'dra bar bya'o//

27a7(rgyud): pa'i mchog ni lag pa gnyis kyis rdo rje'i phyag rgya 'dzin pas rdo rje bzung la ci'i slad du mgul ba de srid du bzlas so// de phyin chad rdo rje des las thams cad byed de//
27b1(rgyud): rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor ro// de nas dam tshig gi dkyil 'khor 'byung ste/ dkyil 'khor chen po kun bris nas/ mtshan ma thams cad bstan par bya// 'jug pa rdo rje dril
27b2(rgyud): bu dang // rdo rje 'dzin mchog phyag rgyas so// de la rdo rje dril bu'i phyag rgya ni 'di yin no// rdo rje 'dzin pa kun byas nas// rdo rjes kun btags par bya'o// g.yas par

27b4(rgyud): tshig kyang // rtag tu bsrungs zhes brjod par bya// ji ltar dril bu'i sgra 'di ni// de'i mi rtag pa ru gsungs// de ltar khyod la rdo rje chen po bde ba zhes bya ba 'di/
27b5(rgyud): nges pa'i bsreg par gyur pa ni// de ste rdo rje 'dzin pa dang // skyabs gsum brtul zhugs de bzhin te// de ltar byang chub sems 'dod rnams/ khyod kyis 'di

27b7(rgyud): nas cho ga bzhin bya'o// dam tshig gi dkyil 'khor ro// de nas las kyi dkyil 'khor 'byung ste// de bzhin dkyil 'khor bris nas su// cha lug mang po bzhag
28a1(rgyud): par tsud// gnas las rnam pa thams cad kyang // slob dpon gyis ni de bzhin bslab// de la las kyi sbyor ba 'di'o// bcom ldan 'das
28a2(rgyud): kyi spyan snga ru zab gru bzhi byas la/ dmar po'i yam shing gis bud la/ dmar po'i me tog 'bras bu rnams sbrang rtsi dang mar la sbag ste/ bla gos g.yas su bzung la
28a3(rgyud): ku shi'i bam po la 'dag ste/ rdo rje'i tshig 'di bzlas shing zhi ba dang / rgyas pa dang dbang du bya ba la sogs pa'i zhi ba'i las rnams la lag pa g.yon pas
28a4(rgyud): bdag gi phyag rgyas bcings te/ g.yas pas bsregs na de dag 'grub par 'gyur ro// bcom ldan 'das kyi rgyab du tha ba gsum du kha ba'i tsher ma rnon po'i
28a5(rgyud): yam shing dang 'dab ma dang / me tog dang yal ga'i rtse mo dang sdong bu dang 'bras bu dang / yang de 'dra ba'i gang gi khrag gis skas nas stan khra bo la 'dag ste/
28a6(rgyud): bla gos g.yon du bzung ba la khros pa'i tshig bzlas shing g.yon pas bsregs na dgug pa dang / bzhug pa dang / bcings pa dang / rgyas gdab pa dang //
28a7(rgyud): gzhom pa dang / bcing ba dang / bskal ba dang / snyom par byas pa dang / gtan po ba la sogs pa'i las dran pa rnams rab tu 'grub par 'gyur ro//
28b1(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dgug pa dang / bzhug pa dang / dam tshig gis bcing ba dang / dbang du bya ba la sogs pa grub pa
28b2(rgyud): thams cad kyi las ni bcom ldan 'das kyi g.yas su rtsa 'jam po gting ba la 'dag ste/ stod g.yogs sbyangs ma ltar gsol to// ting nge 'dzin gyi brlab cing /
28b3(rgyud): 'khor lo lta bu'i thab da du ba med pa'i 'dab ma til dang 'bras la sogs pa nas 'bras g.yas g.yon gyis bsreg go/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyi g.yon du rdo rje
28b4(rgyud): lta bu'i zab byas la stod g.yogs kyi yan lag kun bcing ste/ rlan stan 'jam po la 'dug nas yam shing thabs kyis 'bar ba'i phreng ba la 'dzin pa'i me/ lag
28b5(rgyud): pa g.yas rdo rje dang bcas pa khu tshur gyi phyag rgya bcings nas/ lag pa g.yon pa rdo rje'i khu tshur 'dzin pas bzung nas 'dzum shing dga' bar byas te/ rdo rje'i tshig/
28b6(rgyud): bzlas shing ro thams cad sregs nas/ rdo rje 'dzin pa thams cad dgugs pa dang / bcing ba dang / dbang du bya ba la sogs pa'i dam pa grub pa'i sbyin bsreg gi tshe
28b7(rgyud): ka bya'o// 'jig rten gsum las rnam par rgyal ba'i rtog pa chen po'i rgyal po las dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi cho ga'o// de nas ye byad bshad par bya'o zhes nas
29a1(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin gyis gsungs pa/ dkyil 'khor cho ga thams cad mthong bar 'gyur nas bsgrub po// de ci'i phyir zhe na/
29a2(rgyud): dkyil 'khor ma zhugs sam/ dam tshig spong bar gyur pa ni phyag na rdo rje mi 'grub pa/ gsang ba yang dag ma shes pas/ bcom ldan 'das sems dpa' 'dod
29a3(rgyud): pa/ chags chad rdo rje de nyid do// de la chags par ma gyur na// phyag na rdo rje mi 'grub po// bde bas yang dag ma mthong bas// dkyil 'khor du ni 'grub mi
29a4(rgyud): 'gyur// yang dag ma mthong grub pa ni// the tshom can gyis mi thob po// rab du 'jigs pa rnyed nas su// nad kyis kyang ni 'jigs par byed// gdon kyang
29a5(rgyud): de la brtson par 'gyur// shi nas du 'bod du ni ltung // de ltar dkyil 'khor thams cad du bcug la nad dang gdon la sogs pa ston cig/ bcom ldan 'das
29a6(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa gser gyi kha dog ras la bri bar bya ste/ de'i thad kar ni kun tu byang chub sems dpa' brgyad bri ba ni 'di lta ste/ g.yas phyogs su ni 'phag
29a7(rgyud): pa spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po dang / 'jam dpal dang / sems bskyed ma thag tu chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'o// g.yon phyogs su ni rdo rje khu tshur dang /
29b1(rgyud): byams pa dang nam mkha'i mdzod do// steng du na mkha'i snying po'o// bcom ldan 'das kyi 'og tu ni phyag na rdo rje ste/ rdo rje hUM zhes pa'i phyag na rdo rje dang bcas pa'i
29b2(rgyud): lag pa gnyis kyis bcings pa'o// lag pa gnyis po bzhad pa/ g.yas pa ni rdo rje gsor/ g.yon pas me tog gi gzhu dang mda' lnga bsnams la/ sku mdog
29b3(rgyud): ni ud pa la sngon po lta bu/ yid tsam du 'dzum pa mche ba cung zad rtsigs pa/ khro ba dang bcas pas bzhad pa'i zhal phyir bskyang du gnas pa/ rgyan thams cad
29b4(rgyud): kyis brgyan pa/ zhabs g.yon pas lho chen po'i ldan pa g.yon pa gnan pa/ zhabs g.yas pa bskum pas u ma'i na ma bcings te/ stod g.yogs khra
29b5(rgyud): bos yan lag g.yogs pa/ ko rlon gyi srad g.yogs can/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dbu rgyan du thob pa'o// de nas tshes gcig nas brtsams te tshes
29b6(rgyud): bcwo lnga'i bar ram/ zla ba'i bar ram/ lo'i bar du nyin re bzhin brgya stong bzlas te/ gos dkar po gtsang ma gos te bdag gi khyim du gnas shing / zas gtsang
29b7(rgyud): yid bzhin du zos te bzlas na/ de nas zla ba gcig lon pa dang / zla ba dang pos ni hU~M zhes byas pas phyi rol gyi las rnams 'grub par 'gyur ro// gnyis kyis
30a1(rgyud): ni las thams cad grub par 'gyur ro// gsum gyis ni bcom ldan 'das rmi lam du ston cing 'das pa dang ma 'ongs thams cad ston to//
30a2(rgyud): bzhis ni sems can dgugs pa dang dbang du bya bar nus so// zla ba lngas ni yid bzhin du snang ba dang mi snang bar 'gyur ro// zla ba drug pa ni ci 'dod pa thams cad kyis
30a3(rgyud): gzugs su 'gyur ro// zla ba bdan gyis bdag gis lus sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' dang phyag na rdo rje ston cing cho 'phrul thams cad kyang ston to// zla ba
30a4(rgyud): brgyad kyis stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi lha la sogs pa'i dgugs pa dang bzhag pa dang bcas pa dang dbang du byed cing las su bsgoms so// /
30a5(rgyud): zla ba dgus ni byang chub sems dpa' thams cad dgug pa dang / bzhug pa dang bcings pa dang dbang du byed do// zla ba bcu pa ni sa bcu pa thob par 'gyur ro// zla ba
30a6(rgyud): bcu gcig gis ni sa bcu gcig pa sangs rgyas kyi sa thob bo// zla ba bcu gnyis kyis ni rdo rje 'dzin par 'gyur ro// de nas bsgrub pa bzhin te ras la bcom ldan
30a7(rgyud): 'das rdo rje zhes bya ba de bzhin du bris la/ de'i thad kar thams cad mthu chen po la sogs pa nas/ klu ba ru na'i mthu'i bar du bcom ldan 'das la sgo bzhis pus
30b1(rgyud): mo btsugs pa bris la/ de nas de bzhin du bzlas pa ni hUM zhes pa'i phyag rgya grangs med pa bzlas te/ zla ba'i mtha'i bar du chos nyi shu dgu'i mtshan thal bzlas na nang /
30b2(rgyud): par thams cad 'ong ngo // 'ongs nas kyang dbang du 'gyur// thams cad bsgo ba bzhin du byed do// de nas bslab pa gzhan byung ste bcom ldan 'das de bzhin bris nas
30b3(rgyud): gser mdangs kyi lha mo la sogs pa thams cad rang gi phyag rgyas bsgrengs nas par byed cing mi sdug pa'i gzugs su bri'o// de nas de bzhin du zla ba gcig gi mtha'i
30b4(rgyud): mtshan tha la byung zlos shig/ de nas nang par kun lhag te/ de bzhin du gang dag gi bsgrub pa po mchod do// 'di ni rtog pa 'dir bris pa de bzhin no snyam du
30b5(rgyud): bsams nas des mi 'jigs par bya'o// de nas dpeng du 'gyur te rtag tu las thams cad byed pa'i g.yog mer 'gyur ro// de nas cho ga bzhin te ras la
30b6(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin du bris la/ de nas de bzhin du brgya stong du bzlas nas/ nub tha ma la rdo rje 'dzin pa thob ste ci 'dod pa'i mchog kyang thob po// gzhan yang
30b7(rgyud): sgrub pa phyag na rdo rje'i spyan sngar 'bum bzlas shing de nas dgos kun bcom ldan 'das kyis mdzad do// phyag na rdo rje'i spyan sngararu ci 'dod pa'i lam shing thams cad
31a1(rgyud): kyis sbyin bsreg gis lo gcig gi bar du bsregs na thams cad 'grub par 'gyur ro// de nas rdo rje hUM zhes pa bri ba'i spyan sngar lo gcig
31a2(rgyud): gi mtha'i bar da grangs med par bzlos shing / de nas tha mar bcom ldan 'das rang gi ci 'dod pa'i mchog brtsol bar 'gyur ro// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
31a3(rgyud): gshegs pa'i spyan sngar rdo rje hUM zhes pa'i phyag rgya bcings la de bzhin gshegs pa 'gul gyi bar du zlos shig/ de nas phyag rgya drug par 'gyur ro// grub pa des na
31a4(rgyud): dgug pa dang dbang du bya ba dang / bzhug pa dang drang ba dang / ltung ba dang / dbab pa dang / gtan 'pho ba dang la sogs pa la sa phran sna tshogs kyi rnams bcing bas
31a5(rgyud): hUM zhes bya las mdzad do// de nas cho ga bzhin te reg pas dbang bskur bya bar 'dod na 'dri'am 'dzin pa las phyag rgya rdo rje'i cha lugs byas la phyag rgya gnyis rkyang ste rdo/
31a6(rgyud): rje 'dzin to// de zla ba yar gyi tshes gcig nas brtsams te/ tshes bco lnga'i bar du yang mar bre brgya stong gis khrus shig/ de nas mtha' mar mtshan thal byung bzlas
31a7(rgyud): so// de nas nang par gzugs de bzhin te/ de nas rig pa thams cad kyi bdag po 'gyur ro// de nas bsgrub pa gzhan 'byung ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
31b1(rgyud): kyi cha lug bri ba 'am/ 'dzin pa la de bzhin du phyag rgya skad bod rdo rje 'dzin par byas la// de bzhin gyi bar du spos chus bkru ba na de bzhin yid de bzhin du snang bar
31b2(rgyud): 'gyur ro// de nas sgrub pa gzhan 'byung ste ros la bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje phyag bzhi par byas nas de'i phyag g.yas par pad mo// g.yas par rdo rje hUM zhes
31b3(rgyud): pa/ g.yon par mda' dang gzhu'o// de nas de'i spyan sngar stong phrag brgya bzlas pa'i 'jug tu zhag gsum sbyangs te mtshan thal byung ba bzlas nas/ de'i nang par
31b4(rgyud): de dang 'dra bar gzugs su 'gyur te bskal par gnas shing mi dga' ba dang / sems can thams cad dab de bya ba dang / thams cad du 'gro bar 'gyur ro// de nas
31b5(rgyud): dkyil 'khor bsgrub pa 'byung ste dkyil 'khor mthong ba'i lci bas dus gsum gyis khrus byas dus gsum gyi gos rjes/ rdo rje 'dzin pa'i phyag rgya bcings nas
31b6(rgyud): brgya stong dus gsum du nyin bdun bzlas na/ de nas phyag na rdo rje slob dpon gyi gzugs su byas nas rmi lam du thams cad smra'o// de nas dkyil 'khor bsgrub pa'i
31b7(rgyud): cho gas gzhan 'byung ste dkyil 'khor chen po mthong bas zla ba gcig gi bar du de bzhin du dus gsum du brjod/ dus gsum du ba lang gi lcibs dkyil 'khor
32a1(rgyud): byas te/ rno lcags kyi mtshon las der rdo rje ras la sogs pa 'am/ shing leb la bris nas de la mchod pa byas te/ rdo rje khu tshur gyis bzung
32a2(rgyud): la lo gcig tshun chad rdo rje de nam 'bar ba'i bar du bzlog shig/ 'bar ba des nam mkha' la 'gro ba dang lo bcu drug lon pa'i lus phyag na rdo rje dang mtshungs pa'i
32a3(rgyud): dus gzugs dang stobs dang mdog du 'gyur te/ 'dod pa'i longs spyod thams cad dang ldan pa bde ba dang yid bde ba thams cad thob par 'gyur ro// tshe yang lo
32a4(rgyud): stong phrag brgyar 'gyur ro// de nas ral gri bsgrub pa 'byung ste/ rdo rje khu tshur gi ral gri bzung la lo gcig gi bar da bzlas na rig 'dzin thams cad kyi bdag po rig
32a5(rgyud): 'dzin du 'gyur ro// de nas 'khor lo bsgrub pa 'byung ste/ 'khor lo dkyil 'khor bris la lcags kyi 'khor lo thogs nas nam rdo rjer 'gyur cing slar yang 'khor
32a6(rgyud): lo sgyur ba'i bar du bzlas so// de nas de thags pa ni rig 'dzin thams cad 'khor lo bskor bar 'gyur ro// de nas kyo ba btang bsgrub par 'dod pas phyag na rdo rje'i
32a7(rgyud): spyan sngar gser gyi kyo ba btang byas te lag pa g.yon pa'i rdo rje khu tshur gyis bzung la grub pa rnam gsum du 'gyur bar bzlas te/ dros pa tsam gyis thams cad
32b1(rgyud): 'gug nus par 'gyur ro// du ba byung ba tsam gyis thams cad byed nus par 'gyur ro// 'bar bas ni thams cad dgug pa dang dbang du byas pa nus shing rig
32b2(rgyud): 'dzin gyi rgyal por 'gyur ro// de nas lha la sogs pa thams cad dgag pa 'byung te/ lha chen po la sogs pa lha rnams gang yang rung ba'i cha lugs rkang pa
32b3(rgyud): g.yon pas mnan te/ rdo rje hUM zhes pa'i phyag rgya bcings te/ bsdigs shing zla ba gcig gi mtha'i bar du 'gyur ro// bzlas na thams cad lhags te las thams
32b4(rgyud): cad byed pa'i g.yog tu 'gyur ro// k+Sha dbang du bya bar 'dod na klu'i tshor lte ba man chad chu nang du bcug la ro gcig tshun chad klu thams cad rang gi gzugasu ston cing
32b5(rgyud): las thams cad byed pa'i g.yog tu gyur pa'i bar du bzlas so// gnod sbyin dbang du bya bar 'dod na gnod sbyin gang la gnas pa rdo rje hUM zhes pa'i phyag rgya bcings la
32b6(rgyud): gnod sbyin de dag lhags te ci bka' bstsal ces smras pa'i bar da bzlas so// de phyin chad thams cad byed pa'i g.yog tu 'gyur ro// de nas mi rnams bams
32b7(rgyud): cad dbang du bya bar 'dod pas/ mi'i gnas su song nas khro mo'i snying khar rdog pas mnan la zla ba gcig lon gyi bar du bzlas na ches nyi shu dgu la 'jigs su/
33a1(rgyud): rung ba chen po'i sgra 'byin par byed de/ de nas dbang du gyur nas bka' bzhin byed pa'i g.yog mor 'gyur ro// phrag la khyer nas mtho ris
33a2(rgyud): su khrid de slar yang khrid cing 'ongs nas tshogs kyi bdag por bcug cing de dag gis mchod de sngon ma byung ba'i don thams cad dang / 'dod pa thams cad dang / na chung
33a3(rgyud): thams cad dgug go/ 'di lta bu'i rnal 'byor ste te/ rnal 'byor gyis khro bo'i 'jig rten du yang 'gro zhing phyir 'ongs // de la su cung zad kyang byed mi nus so//
33a4(rgyud): de nas dpal chen mo 'grub par phyag na rdo rje'i spyan sngar bzlas pa ni phyag na rdo rje sku las lha mo'i lus mthong gi ba ra da ste/ de las ma 'gul cig ces bsgo/ de byin
33a5(rgyud): chad don thams cad ster bar 'gyur te/ sangs rgyas pa yang ster ba'i bar du'o// de nas mtsho dbyangs ma dbaded bya bar 'dod nas/ de nas phyag na rdo rje'i
33a6(rgyud): spyan sngar yi ge'i phreng bar byas la phreng ba'i yi ge bkod cing mthar byin gyi bar blags te/ nyin re bzhin dus gsum du las de byas la de nas brgya stong bzlas na
33a7(rgyud): zla ba gcig lon pa dang mtsho dbyangs ma mthong ngo // de phyin chad thogs pa med pa'i spobs pa dang ldan par 'gyur ro// 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa/
33b1(rgyud): dang thams cad kyi btsug lag thams cad shes gnyen du bya bar thams cad dang / bzo thams cad dang ma bslabs par de ltar rab tu shes so// de nas lig bu mig
33b2(rgyud): dang gur bum dang / ldong ros dang ba blang rnams la sgrub pa 'byung ste/ ling bug blangs la 'dzom pa'i steng du bzhag nas lag pas mnan te grub pa rnam pa gsum 'byung
33b3(rgyud): gi bar du bzlas so// gcig gis ni mi snang bar 'gyur ro// gnyis pas ni gzugs mang por 'gyur ro// gsum pas ni nam gnas gong mar 'dzegs pas na mkha'
33b4(rgyud): la 'gro bar 'gyur ro// gur gum la sogs pa bzung ste/ 'jom pa'i bu gang bcug la rdo rje 'dzin pa'i phyag rgyas mnan nas nam mkha' 'bar gyi bar da bzlas so//
33b5(rgyud): de nas thig le byas nas 'dod pa thams cad kyi bdag po dang rig 'dzin dang thams cad du 'gro ba dang / tsho lo stong thub par 'gyur ro// de nas sa la b+han dzi ka bsgrub
33b6(rgyud): pa 'byung ste gnas gang las bAn dza ka'i ri mo bris pa 'am/ gzugs su byas pa de'i 'jom pa la sor mo bzhag ste zla ba gcig tu bzlas so// de nas zla ba gcig
33b7(rgyud): gi mthar mtshan thog thag du bzlos shig/ de nas nang par gzugs su ston nas 'dod pa thams cad sbyin pa'i chung mar 'gyur ro// gnod sbyin mo bsgrub par 'dod
34a1(rgyud): pas gnod sbyin mo gang na 'dug pa'i gnas der 'dug pa rang gi gzugs su 'ongs kyi bar du bzlas na de la 'dod pa thams cad ster ba'i
34a2(rgyud): bran mor 'gyur ro// de nas sha za mo bslab par 'dod pas brag phug logs su me btang ste/ lag pa g.yon pas rang gi mtshan de bzung la g.yas pas gzegs ma
34a3(rgyud): bsregs pa ni phyag dang gi phung po de las ci tsam na sha za mo gdongs mangs gzugs mi sdug pa'o// de ste rang gi gzugs su gnas so// de yang de bzhin du bran mor
34a4(rgyud): 'gyur ro// de nas ci bgyi ba bslab par 'dod pas nyin zhag gcig sbyang bar byas la tshes nyi shu dgu la brgya stong bzlas te/ de nas zla ba gcig slong mo la za zhing grangs
34a5(rgyud): med par bzlas te zla ba gcig lon pa dang / na pa gsum sbyang ba byas mtshan thog thag bzlas so// de nas nang par ci bgyi 'dod na des mi 'jigs par byas te de nas
34a6(rgyud): derang gnas 'grub po// de byin chad 'dod pa thams cad 'bul ba'i g.yob tu 'gyur ro// mabo ris kyi lha mo yang dgug cing 'bul lo// de yang skyel cing slar
34a7(rgyud): yang 'gug go// 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar gyi thams cad smra'o// gzhan gyi nor thams cad kyang phrogs nas 'bul le// de nas rig pa'i rtul zhugs/
34b1(rgyud): bya bar 'dod pa dngos grub med pa gang yin pa des zla ba drug gi bar du nyin zhags bcu bzhi spyod pa snga ma rjes la srong me'i kha zas la sogs pa nas rlung bzung ba'i
34b2(rgyud): bar da'o// de nas 'jug tu mtshan thal byung bzlas na nang par sangs rgyas la sbyin par 'gyur ro// de nas nyin re bzhin bcwo brgyad kyi bar du sngon du spyad pa rnams
34b3(rgyud): de'i 'jug tu mtshan thal byung bzlas na nang par las thams cad grub par 'gyur ba ni hUM zhes thang cig pas kyang ngo // de nas ro langs bsgrub par 'gyur te/ ma smad
34b4(rgyud): ma nyams pa'i mo ro blangs la legs par bkrus nas byugs te me tog phreng ba btags nas rkang pa g.yon pas mnan te dbugs kyi bar du bzlas na de ldang ste langs
34b5(rgyud): pa dang de zhon nas thams cad du 'gro zhing tshe yang stong phrag brgyar 'gyur ro// de nas ro langs kyi grub pa mchog bsgrub pa 'byung ste/ ma smas ma nyams pa'i mi ro
34b6(rgyud): langs nas de bzhin du rab tu brgyan pa zhon te langs zhing yang 'gyel gyi bar du bzlas na de bzhin gshegs pa'i skar 'gyur ro// phrag pa la khyer na de bzhin gshegs
34b7(rgyud): pa thams cad 'phel ba'i rig 'dzin 'jig rten gyi khams rab 'byams thams cad du 'phrul gyi 'gro ba dang / tshe yang bskal par 'gyur ro zhes bcom ldan 'das phyag/
35a1(rgyud): na rdo rje la gsungs pa'o// de nas bsgrubs kyang dkyil 'khor mthong ba nyid kyis las su 'gyur ba ni 'di lta ste/ zang cig brjod pas ni
35a2(rgyud): bdag dang grong khyer dang / rgyal po la sogs pa bsrung bar 'gyur ro// 'tshams bcad pa la sogs pa ni brtan par ltas pas 'tshams bcad na de bzhin gshegs pa
35a3(rgyud): thams cad kyang mi 'da' na gzhan lta ci smos/ sa'i dkyil 'khor dang nam mkha' dang phyogs bcing ba blta ba des so// dbab pa ni rig pa dang ma rig pas ral gri dang
35a4(rgyud): me long dang / snod dang the bo dang / shing ljon pa dang bris pa dang cha lugs dang / gzha dang mda' dang rdo rje la sogs pa rdo rje dbab pa'i phyag rgya gos kyis g.yogs pa
35a5(rgyud): bcing ste gu gul gyi gdag pas btab po// gdon zhi bar bya ba ni hUM zhes pas so// rdo rje hUM zhes pa'i phyag rgyas ni sems can thams cad 'phyang bar byed do// rdo rje sgrog
35a6(rgyud): gi phyag rgyas ni byed ma'i gdon las thar bar byed do// he ru ka rdo rje'i phyag rgya bstan pa ni byad mas bsad pa las slar gse'i bar bya'o// rdo rje'i phyag rgya bzung la/ skra
35a7(rgyud): la bzung ste bslangs pas ni dug gi zhi ba dang gnan pa dang dug bslang ba dang / dug zhi bar bya ba dang / dug sos pa dang / dug bshig par bya ba dang / dug gis shi ba
35b1(rgyud): las bso bar byas ste rdo rje ts+tsha zhes pa cig gis so// gter byung ba ni zangs kyi ril pa chus bkang ba la rdo rje hU~M zhes pa'i 'dzub mo bu gul gyi bdug par bya ste bzlas te gter/
35b2(rgyud): yod na ni chu lud do// de ste med na ni 'khyil lo// de nas 'jig rten gsum las rnam par rgyal ba'i hA zhes bzlas te blang ngo // snang la dbug pa'i gdong ka ljon pa'i
35b3(rgyud): yam shing gi sa mes bus te zho dang sbrang rtsi mar gyis ra dza ko shing ta ka'i me tog la sngags bskas te stong phrag brgyad bsregs pa na snang ba thob pa'i 'og gis gnas su rdo rje
35b4(rgyud): 'og gi phyag rgyas 'khrul 'khor thams cad bcom ldan 'das rdo rje hUM zhes pa'i bzlas te zhogs na de las sus kyang rtse bar mi nus so// gtog 'dod kyi 'khor los
35b5(rgyud): kyang ci yang byed par mi 'gyur ro// phyag na rdo rje'i spyan sngar rdo rje 'am/ nor bu 'am/ ma na ti'i pad ma ra ga 'am mu tig gam/ gser ram dbyig gam gzhan ci yang rung ba
35b6(rgyud): 'am/ skyes pa 'am bud med dam/ sangs rgyas kyi sku gzugs la lo gcig gi bar da dus gsum du brgyar bzlas na lo gcig lon nas brgyar 'gyur ro// de snyed pa
35b7(rgyud): brgyar bzlas na de snyed brgyar 'gyur ro// de nas stong du bzlas na yang stong gsum du 'gyur ro// longs spyod dgug pa ni stong phrag brgyad bzlas so// dgug pa ni rdo rje kye ba
36a1(rgyud): takyi phyag rgyas bzla ba bzhis zhugs so// dbang du bya ba ni rdo rje khu tshur gyi dam tshig gi phyag rgyas so// sems can thams cad rten 'pho ba ni
36a2(rgyud): hA zhes pa'i phyag rgya bcings te stong phrag brgyar bzlas na sems can yid kyis dmigs bzhin btan pa'o// chu mnan pa ni phyag rgyas bcings la chu'i steng du 'gror

36b5(rgyud): gson no// gang 'phrogs pa ni rang gi lce sos bzung nas hUM zhes pa'i bar sbyor bar bya'o// snying drang ba ni rdo rje sor mo'i phyag rgyas dpung pa snol te rang gi mtshan gzhang

51b1(rgyud): can thams cad dbang du 'gyur ro// lkugs pa'i rtul zhugs kyis 'bum bzlas na tshogs thams cad kyi dbang du 'gyur ro// bud med kyi yin na 'dzom par rtogs gtsugs te

73a1(rgyud): ces bya'o// mnyam par bzhag pas ting nge 'dzin/ nges pas rdo rje nyid du 'gyur/ de la smras pa sems gzugs med pa la ji ltar sra ba'i rdo rjer 'gyur/
73a2(rgyud): smras pa ji ltar rnam par shes pa las sems can skye ba na sha dang rus pa 'byung bar 'gyur ba zhig ste/ sdug pa dang chags pa dang bde ba dang / rnam par shes pa gzugs med
73a3(rgyud): pa rnams 'das pa las sems can skye ba dang / ji ltar klu rnams khros po'i sems kyis ting nge 'dzin nges par nam mkha' las gnam lcags 'byung ba'am/ glog dang bcas

73a5(rgyud): rje de nyid ni bsgoms pas sems dpa' nyid du 'gyur ro// de la sems dpa' byin gyis brlabs pa sbyor ba gang zhe na/ sems dpa' kun gyi bdag ce na bdag nyid la yang
73a6(rgyud): gnas so zhes byin gyis brlab nas sems can bdag yin zhes nga rgyal bsgom par bya/ de nyid bcom ldan 'ad sems dpa' ste/ rdo rje sems dpa' rgyal ba yin// sang

73b1(rgyud): rigs kyang de nyid de// de ni rdo rje 'chang ba'i rigs// de nyid spyan ras gzigs kyi rigs// de nyid nor bu'i rigs yin te// khams gsum de nyid yin zhes gsungs/

73b3(rgyud): ba'i mgon po ste// gnas pa dang rim gro pa yin zhes bcom ldan 'das thog ma dang tha ma med pa'i sems dpa' phyag na rdo rjes gsungs so// de kho na nyid chen po'i bar

73b6(rgyud): de nas phyag rgya'i khyad par ni rdo rje'i sku gsungs thugs rnams kyis/ gzugs brnyan sbyor ba 'di dag ni phyag rgya'i kun gyis khyab par ste/ 'byung ba yang ni de yi bstan/
73b7(rgyud): ji ltar jo bo'i byab rgya mthong na/ bran rnams 'gal ba mi byed pa// de bzhin rgyal ba nyid rnams kyang // phyag rgya 'da' bar yongs mi mdzad// do rje sku dang gsung dang bugs

74a3(rgyud): pa'i rgyu yi mchog/ gang gis thams cad lus bstan 'gyur// de phyir phyag rgya brjod pa yin// gang gis thams cad rgyas btab pa// chud mi za zhing rab spang ste// mnga' bdag

74a7(rgyud): 'di lta ste// ma rig pa ni med par byed// rig pa de bzhin chud par byed// don rnams rtogs par 'gyur bas na// rig pa zhes ni de phyir bya// snying po dang phyag rgya dang
74b1(rgyud): sngags dang rig pa'i bar tu bya ba gnyis so// de nas phyag rgya bcings pa'i rab tu bya ba bshad do zhes bcom ldan 'das bla na med pa'i phyag rgya thams cad kyi ye shes rdo rje 'dzin pas
74b2(rgyud): gsungs so// de la phyag rgya chen po ni de nyid bskul ba'i snying pos bcings so// dam tshig dang las kyi phyag rgya ni rdo rje bcings pa dang / brdab pa la sogs pa byas nas bcing //

74b4(rgyud): med pa la mi sbyin no// yun du skyabs gnas de dag kyang 'grub par 'gyur ro// de la kho na bskal pa'i snying po 'di'o// sa ma ya snyom/ de la dam tshig chen po'i kho na bskal
74b5(rgyud): ba'i snying po ni 'di yin no// sa ma ya ho su ra te snyom rdo rje 'gro bas phyag rgya thams cad rang gis bcing ngam/ gzhan 'ching du bzhag na ni hUM zhes pa thang cig tsam gyis so//

75a1(rgyud): badz+ra muSh+Ta/ zhes brjod pas bcing ngo // de nas phyag rgya thams cad bcing ngo // de ste de ltar ma byas na yang / sa ma ya snyom zhes brjod la phyag rgya

75a5(rgyud): tu bsdams pa ni rdo rje bcing ba'o// de nyid mthe chung dang srin lag gi bar du bcug la btsum pa 'dis ni rjes su dbab pa'i dam tshig gi phyag rgya'o// de nyid las mthe bo gnyis gshib

75b1(rgyud): phyag rgya bcing ngo // lha'i phyag rgya ni snying po'i don gyis bcing ngo // se'i phyag rgya dang mchu'i mig bsgral ba'i phyag rgya dang / snying po dang / lus g.yo ba'i phyag rgya ni/ sa ma ya/

75b3(rgyud): khro bo'i 'dzub mo zhes bya ba yin no// rdo rje khro bo'i 'drub mo gnyis lag ngar bsngal de bcings nas kyang mthe chung lcags kyus sbrel byas nas/ hU~M zhes pas sdigs par bya/

109a3(rgyud): bya'o// gdug cing khros pa dgas pa la ni khros pas lcags phye'i sprin bsregs gis so// bdud thams cad brlag par bya ba la ni rang gis sa bon gyis sbyin bsreg giso//
109a4(rgyud): gnod sprin thams cad bskrad pa la ni ha ha zhes rgod cing bzlos paso// klu thams cad gdon pa la ni rdo rje sa la brdebs shing bzlas pas so// lha rnams ltung bar bya ba la ni lha mo rdo rje

109a6(rgyud): rnam thos sras rjes su 'brang bar bya ba la ni rnam thos sras mnan nas khros pas bzlas brjod bya'o// lus ngan po mnan nas dpal 'phrog pa la ni rdo rje skyes bus so// 'dod pa'i lha dbang
109a7(rgyud): du bya ba la ni 'dod pa'i lha'i mdun du khros pas bzlas brjod bya'o// tshangs pa ltung bar bya ba la ni rdo rje rab tu dga' ba'i phyag rgyas so// khyab 'jug gzhig pa la ni rdo rje 'khor lo dral/
109b1(rgyud): ba so// dbang phyug chen po gdul ba la ni rdo rje tri shul dral bas so// ma mo thams bsad pa la ni rdo rje khro bo'i tshogs kyi srin mos so// phyi'i dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi phyag rgya dang / dam

109b4(rgyud): khro bo'i rta ba'i mig la reg paso// ltung ba thams cad bslang ba la ni rdo rje khro bo'i spang ba so// thams cad spo ba la ni rdo rje khro bo'i rnal 'byor mas so// thams cad dbrog pa la ni
109b5(rgyud): rdo rje khro bo'i khu tshur gyis so// 'jig pa thams cad bskyed pa la ni rdo rje khro bo'i lta bas so// dpung thams cad bsad pa la ni rdo rje khro bo'i gnod sbyin mas so// gzhan gyi dpung
109b6(rgyud): thams cad gzhom pa dang // gnod pa dang / rmongs par bya ba dang / long bar bya ba dang / rgyas gdab pa/ gsad pa la ni rdo rje khro bo ma rungs pa'i sngon mos so// rgyal po la sog
109b7(rgyud): pa mi chen po thams cad gas pa la ni dong ka'i shing la rang gi khrag gi sbyin bsreb byas pas so// lha thams cad rnam par gzhig pa la ni sgra thams cad kyi gzugs brnyan gyi lam shis

110b3(rgyud): gang la la shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul 'di nyan pa dang / 'dzin pa dang / klog pa dang / bsgom pa de 'dod chags dang / dri ma thams cad kyi nang na 'dug kyang / pad mo lta bur
