116a1(rgyud): sems can thams cad bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpa' phyag rgya thams cad kyis rdo rje sems dpa' nyid du de bzhin gshegs pa thad
116a2(rgyud): la sogs pa dngos grub mchog gi rgyud rgyas btab po// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje khu tshur gyis yang skra dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje thams cad la phyag rgya chen po pa la sogs
116a3(rgyud): pa phyag rgya thams cad kyi dam tshig gi sems dpa' phyung nas// dang po dkyil 'khor gyi tshul gyis bzhugs par gyur to// de bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje khu tshur
116a4(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes kyi phyag rgya'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas// phyag rgya thams cad kyi rdo rje'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i
116a5(rgyud): dkyil 'khor chen po 'di gsungs so// phyi'i dkyil 'khor dang po'i sbyor bas bris la nang du rdo rje ga thig gi 'khor lo bri'o// de bzhin du 'di dbus su dkyil 'khor brgyad
116a6(rgyud): par thig btab la/ dbus su bcom ldan 'das rdo rje khu tshur phyag gnyis dam tshig gi phyag rgya bcings la/ zhal rnam par bzhad pa bzhag go// de'i mdun du rdo rje sku'i mchog ces
116a7(rgyud): khyab rdo rje bsnyems pa 'dzin pa'o// g.yas su rdo rje sngags zhes bya ba rdo rje sde'i mchog 'dzin pa'o// rgyab du ting nge 'dzin zhes bya ba rdo rje 'dzidi pa'o// g.yon du rdo rjezhes bya ba bam/
116b1(rgyud): pa 'dzin pa'o// lho'i mtshams su phyag rgya'i khu chur bya ba dang / gnyis pa la ni nor bu khu tshur zhes bya ba dang / gsum pa ni chos kyi khu tshur zhes bya ba dang / bzhi pa la ni las kyi khwa/
116b2(rgyud): chur zhes bya ba rang gi phyag rgya dang / phyag mtshan yang 'dzin par bya'o// sgo rnams su ni rdo rje bsnyems pa la sogs pa'i phyag rgya'i lha mo rnams bri bar bya'o// de nas dam tshig gi phyag rgya
116b3(rgyud): yongs su bzung ba rang nyid zhugs nas phyag rgya thams cad kyi slob dpon du 'gyur ro// de nas brtsams te dngos grub thams cad don yod par 'thob par 'gyur ro// de nas tham cad
116b4(rgyud): kyi ye shes kyi dbang phyug tu bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs byang chub tu myur bar rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ro// der zhugs nas phyag rgya bcings pa bcom ldan 'das
116b5(rgyud): lus bslab pa bya zhing / rdo rje ming gis dbang bskur 'di skad brjod par bya'o// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje yi/ gzugs brnyan lta bur sbyor ba yi/ phyag rgya kun ces bya ba bsgrab/
116b6(rgyud): dam tshig dngos grub ster ba'o// slob ma bzhugs pa'ang de bzhin no// phyag rgya thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor ro// bsgrub pa dang dngos grub kyang de bzhin no// de nas ma grub
116b7(rgyud): ba'i las rnams kyang de bzhin te// phyag rgya thams cad bcing ba bsgrub pa la// snying khar rdo rje khu tshur gyis so// phyag rgya thams cad bsgrub pa la ni rdo rje chen po'i khu tshur gyis so//
117a1(rgyud): thams cad bsgrub pa la ni rdo rje 'dzin pa'i khu tshur gyis so// rang nyid 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar gyi dngos go
117a2(rgyud): rnams ston pa la ni rdo rje ljags kyi mchog gi khru tshur gyis so// rdo rje 'dzin pa nyid la na rdo rje bsnyems pa'i khu tshur gyis so// sangs rgyas nyid la ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
117a3(rgyud): kyi rdo rje'i khu tshur gyis so// bde ba chen po rdo rje don yod pa'i dam tshig gi rtog pa'i rgyal po chen po las/ phyag rgya thams cad kyi khu tshur gyi dam tshig ces bya ba rtog pa'i rgyal po chen
117a4(rgyud): po rdzogs s+ho// / de nas bcom ldan 'das chos thams cad spros pa med pa'i de bzhin gshegs pas yang 'khor lo ltar yi gis bskor ba zhes bya
117a5(rgyud): ba/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul 'di bshad de/ ngo bo nyid med pa'i tshul gyis chos thams cad stong pa'o// mtshan ma med pa'i tshul gyis chos thams cad mtshan ma med
117a6(rgyud): ba'o// smon pa med pa'i tshul gyis chos thams cad mtshan ma med pa'o// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su dag pas chos thams cad rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba'o//
117a7(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa don 'di nyid rgya cher ston te/ bzhin 'dzum bzhin du ral gri des/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la 'debs shing
117b1(rgyud): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i snying po'i mchog 'di gsungs so// a de nas 'di gsungs pa tsam gyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad 'dus par mdzad nas/ dang po'i
117b2(rgyud): dkyil 'khor gyi tshul gyis bzhugs so// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa chos thams cad ngo bo nyid med pas spros pa med pa'i ral gri zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms
117b3(rgyud): par zhugs nas/ 'khor lo ltar yi ges bskor ba zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor gsungs so// phyi'i dkyil 'khor ji lta ba'i nang du 'khor lo bris la/ a la sogs pa'i yi
117b4(rgyud): ge'i phreng ba go ribs bzhin du bri bar bya'o// de nas dkyil 'khor brgyad pa'i tshul gyi thig btab la/ de'i lte ba la bcom ldan 'das/ 'jam napal gzhon nu/ gzhon
117b5(rgyud): na'i cha lugs 'chang zhing 'dzum pa dang bcas par na mkha'i mdog can phyag bzhi dang ral gris de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la 'debs par bzhag par bya'o// de'i mdun la sog
117b6(rgyud): par de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku rnams bzhag par bya'o// phyi'i mtshams rnams su she rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bzhi lung ji lta ba bzhin du bzhag par bya'o// sgo rnams su ni mtshan
117b7(rgyud): ma bzhi bzhag par bya'o// 'di lta ste/ ral gri dang / mdung dang / lhung bzed dang / glegs bam rnams so// de nas ral gri dang thebs bam gyi phyag rgyas de bzhin
118a1(rgyud): du chos kyi slob dpon du byin gyis brlabs so// de nas ral gri blangs te// ral gri ming gi dbang bskur la// chos 'di skad bshad par bya ste/
118a2(rgyud): ral gri 'di ni rtag tu bzung // she rab tshul 'di skar ma bzhing // na mkha' sangs rgyas sbyor ba yis// 'debs na myur du 'grub par 'gyur// sangs rgyas bstan pa bsrung phyir dang /
118a3(rgyud): 'di bsang sdig par mi 'gyur zhing // bsod nams dag kyang thob par 'gyur// slob ma la'ang de bzhin te/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs pa'i dngos grub rnam kyis
118a4(rgyud): myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ro// chos kyi dkyil 'khor bsgrub pa yang de bzhin no// ma bsgrubs par yang de bzhin
118a5(rgyud): du las rnams grub par 'gyur ba ni stong pa nyid kyi ting nge 'dzin thob lnga ni thams cad na mkha' bsgobs pas so// mtshan ma med pa'i ting nge 'dzin thob pa la ni mtshan ma dang bral ba'i
118a6(rgyud): ting nge 'dzin bsgoms pas so// smon pa med pa'i ting nge 'dzin thob pa la ni smon pa med pa bsgoms pas so// rang bzhin gyi 'od gsal ba'i chos kyi ye shes pa la ni shes rab kyi pha rol
118a7(rgyud): phyin pa bsgoms pas so// nyon mongs pa thams cad gcod pa la ni chos bsgoms pas so// yi ge thams cad nges pa'i tshig gi yi ge shes pa la ni spros pa med pa'i ye shes bsgoms pas
118b1(rgyud): gnas thams cad du yi ge chos kyi bya ba mthong ba la ni a la sogs pa yi ge'i ngo bo nyid bsgoms pas so// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byang chub thob pa la ni rdo rje ral gri'i phyag
118b2(rgyud): rgyas so// bde ba chen po rdo rje don yod pa'i dam tshig gi rtog pa'i rgyal po chen po las/ 'khor lo chen po ltar yi ge bskor ba'i dam tshig ces bya ba rtog pa'i rgyal po las/ 'khor lo chen po
118b3(rgyud): ltar yi ge bskor ba'i dam tshig ces bya ba rtog pa'i rgyal po chen po rdzogs s+ho// // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
118b4(rgyud): 'khor lo'i nang du 'dus pa'i de bzhin gshegs pas yang 'khor lo chen po la 'jug pa zhes bya ba/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di bshad do// rdo rje mnyam pa nyid la 'jug pa ni de
118b5(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor la 'jug par 'gyur ro// don gyi mnyam pa nyid la 'jug pa ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i 'khor lo// 'jug par
118b6(rgyud): 'gyur ro// chos thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid la 'jug pa ni dam pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo la 'jug par 'gyur ro// thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid la 'jug pa ni 'khor lo thams cad
118b7(rgyud): la 'jug par 'gyur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems bskyed ma thag tu chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba chos nyid kyi don 'di rgya cher ston cing bzhin rab tu 'dzum nas/ rdo rje 'khor lo/
119a1(rgyud): bskor zhing / rdo rje 'khor lo thams cad 'dzum pa'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i snying po 'di smras so// hUM/ de nas 'di gsungs pa tsam gyis
119a2(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po can khams gsum du gtogs pa'i sems can thams cad dkyil 'khor thams cad du zhugs nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs las
119a3(rgyud): dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi dam tshig gi sems dpa' rnams nges par byung nas dkyil 'khor gyi tshul gyis ji lta ba bzhin du bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems
119a4(rgyud): dpa' sems dpa' rdo rje 'khor lo thams cad la rab tu 'jug pa'i phyag rgya zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ dkyil 'khor chen po thams cad du 'jug pa'i dam tshig
119a5(rgyud): ces bya ba'i 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor 'di gsungs so// phyi'i dkyil 'khor ji lta ba bzhin du bya ste/ nang gi dkyil 'khor du rdo rje 'khor lo bri sa la/ dbus su rdo rje'i 'khor lo'i
119a6(rgyud): 'khor lo bskor ba bzhag par bya'o// phyag rgyan rdo rje la sogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' thams cad rnam pa thams cad du dkyil 'khor dang po'i tshul du bzhug par bya'o//
119a7(rgyud): phyi'i mtshams rnams su rdo rje rigs kyi dkyil 'khor ba'i bri bar bya'o// sgo rnams su ni mtshan ma bzhi bzhag par bya ste/ 'di lta ste/ rdo rje sems dpa'i sku dang / rdo rje khro bar/
119b1(rgyud): skra dang / sran ras gzigs dbang phyug gi sku dang / na mkha'i snying po'i sku rnams so// de nas rdo rje 'khor lo'i phyag rgyas ji lta ba bzhin du dkyil 'khor thams cad du sangs rgyas
119b2(rgyud): nyid dang / rdo rje sems dpa' nyid 'grub par 'gyur ro// de nas 'khor lo blangs la 'khor lo'i ming gis dbang bskur ba ni gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor bzhi'i thig btab pa'i/
119b3(rgyud): rigs rnams su 'jug par bya'o// slob ma bzhugs pa yang de bzhin no// 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor ro// bsgrub pa yang de bzhin no// ma bsgrubs pa yang dkyil 'khor
119b4(rgyud): du 'jug pa la ni rdo rje 'khor lo ste/ rang gi khar bcug la bzhag par bya'o// dkyil 'khor chen por 'jug pa la ni rdo rje 'khor lo chen pos so// de bzhin du phyag rgya'i dkyil 'khor du
119b5(rgyud): 'jug pa la ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor lo'i phyag rgyas so// de bzhin du dam tshig gi dkyil 'khor du 'jug pa la ni dam tshig chen po'i 'khor los so// las kyi dkyil
119b6(rgyud): 'khor du zhugs pa la ni rdo rje thams cad kyis 'khor los so// de bzhin du rjes su chags pa bya ba dang / dbang du bya ba dang / don thob pa dang / rgyas gdab pa dang / bcad pa dang /
119b7(rgyud): mchod pa dang / gdub pas 'dul ba'i las rnams ni sems dpa' chen po brgyad kyi phyag rgya g.yon na 'khor lo dang bcas pa rnams so// bde ba chen po rdo rje don yod pa dam tshig go/
120a1(rgyud): rtog pa'i rgyal po chen po las/ dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi rdo rje dam tshig ces bya ba rtog pa'i rgyal po rdzogs s+ho//
120a2(rgyud): / de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la mchod pa thams cad kyi cho ga rgyas pa bsnod kyi mchod pa thams cad kyi mchog ces bya ba
120a3(rgyud): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul 'di bshad do// byang chub kyi sems bskyed pa nyid ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mchod pa'i cho ba rgyas pa'o// sems can gyi khams thad
120a4(rgyud): yongs su skyob pa nyid ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mchod pa'i cho ga rgyas pa'o// dam pa'i chos yongs su 'dzin pa ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la mchod pa'i cho ga rgyas
120a5(rgyud): pa'o// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yi ge 'bri ba dang / yi ge 'brir 'jug pa dang / 'dzin pa dang / klog pa dang / brjod pa dang / ston pa dang / nyan pa dang / sems dpa'
120a6(rgyud): dang / bsgom pa dang / mchod pa byed pa ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la mchod pa'i cho ga rgyas pa'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po na mkha'i marjod do de/
120a7(rgyud): nyid rgya cher ston te/ bzhin rab tu 'dzum zhing las thams cad don yod pa'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i snying po 'di smras so// oM de nas 'di gsungs pa tsam gyis na mkha'i thams
120b1(rgyud): cad las mchod pa thams cad kyi cho ga rgyas pa na mkha'i khams ma lus pa spros par gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das na mkha'i mdzod kyi byang chub sems dpa'i tshul gyis dkyil 'khor chen po'i/
120b2(rgyud): tshul du zhugs so// de nas byang chub sems dpa' na mkha'i mdzod mchod pa thams kyi cho ga rgyas pa byin gyis brlabs pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ rdo rje'i mchod
120b3(rgyud): pa'i mchog don yod pa'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i dkyil 'khor 'di gsungs so// phyi'i dkyil 'khor ji lta ba la de bzhin du nang du rin po che'i ka ba brgyad byas pa/ dbus su bcom ldan 'das
120b4(rgyud): mtshon cha sna tshogs 'dzin pa/ zhal 'dzum pa/ sku dang yan lag zla ba'i mdog la sogs pa'i kha dog lnga'i mdog can bzhag par bya'o// de'i thams cad du dam tshig sems dpa' rnam bzhag par bya'o//
120b5(rgyud): 'jig rten dbang phyug la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' brgyad po byang chub sems dpa' ting nge 'dzin dang / dbang bskur ba dang / phyag rgya yongs su 'dzin pa dang / stong pa nyid du smra ba dang /
120b6(rgyud): dkyil 'khor 'dri ba dang / mchod pa thams cad dang / sems can thams cad yongs su skyob pa ni bla na med pa'i mchod pa'i cho ga rgyas pa phyag rgya yongs su 'dzin pa'i tshul gyis ji lta ba bzhin du bzhi'o//
120b7(rgyud): phyi'i mtshams rnams su me tog la sogs pa rnams dang / sgo rnams su ni dbyig dang / gser dang / mu tig dang / rin po che ste/ mtshan ma bzhi bzhag par bya'o// de nas de bzhin du rdo rje
121a1(rgyud): @thams cad kyi mchod pa thams cad thob par 'gyur ro// zhugs nas sna tshogs rdo rje blangs nas/ sna tshogs rdo rje'i ming gi dbang bskur nas/ mchod pa rnam pa pani
121a2(rgyud): byas ste/ 'di lta ste/ lus kyis las thams cad kyi phyag bya ba dang / ngag dang / yid dang / sems kyis chos kyi dbyings su spros pas/ mchod pa'i cho ga rgyas pa thams cad kyis
121a3(rgyud): mchod par bya zhing / rdo rje dang phyag rgyas mchod pas gcig tu byas pa'o// slob ma rnams bzhug pa'i cho ga'ang de bzhin no// las kyi dkyil 'khor ro// de nas bsgrub pa dang dngos
121a4(rgyud): grub dag kyang de bzhin no// de nas ma bsgrubs pa yang byang chub kyi sems kyi mchod pa la ni rang gi snying khar rdo rje bsgom pas so// ting nge 'dzin gyi mchod pa la ni thams cad dag par bsgo/

121b2(rgyud): kyi khu tshur yongs su 'dzin pa sems can thams cad 'dul ba'i ye shes kyi snying po zhes bya ba shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul 'di bshad do// sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid
121b3(rgyud): pa khro bo mnyam pa nyid do// sems can thams cad 'dul ba nyid pas khro bo 'dul ba nyid do// sems can thams cad chos nyid pas khro ba chos nyid do// sems can thams cad
121b4(rgyud): rdo rje nyid pas khro ba rdo rje nyid do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar sems can thams cad 'dul ba'i byang chub po// de nas byang chub sems dpa' bdud kyi stobs thams cad rab tu

122a1(rgyud): @bya ba'i gnod sprin gyi dkyil 'khor 'di gsungaso// phyi'i dkyil 'khor tshul du ni// phyi'i dkyil 'khor bri bar bya// de ni sa nang rims nyid du
122a2(rgyud): ni dkyil 'khor bzang po gru bzhi pa// sgo bzhi pa la thig bzhir ldan// mtshon sna lngas ni rnam par bris// ka ba brgyad kyi mdun gnas par/ 'bar ba'i dkyil 'khor yang dag
122a3(rgyud): ldan// de'i dbus su ci rigs par/ rdo rje gnod sbyin bzhag bya ste// rdo rje mche ba rtsigs pa dang / 'bar ba'i phreng ba 'khrigs pa'i 'od// 'jigs byed kha dog sngo ba dang /
122a4(rgyud): ha ha zhes gzhad gsal ba'i zhal/ de yi kun tu gnod sbyin ni// shin tu 'jigs pa bzhag par bya/ de nyid dang po la sogs mchog/ phyag na rdo rje sogs mtshan 'chang // phyi yi

122b1(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad bsrung ba/ gnod sbyin gyi bdag po chen po phyag rdo rje gtum po'i bdag grub pa yin no zhes shes par bya'o// de nas phyag thams cad bcing bar bya zhing bsgrub par

122b4(rgyud): po ji lta ba bzhin no// gdag pa thams cad 'dul ba ni rdo rje mche ba'i phyag rgyas so// sems can thams cad 'dul ba ni khro bas ha ha zhes rgod cing bzhag paso// rang sangs rgyas
122b5(rgyud): 'dod chags dang bral ba la ni ltung bar bya ba ni chos gos dang rnams sbyar gyi sbyin sreg gis so// dbang bskur ba thams cad dbrog pa la ni thams cad phye ma'i sprin bsreg gis so//

252a1(rgyud): gi phyag rgya'i rgyud ni/ pad ma chen po rdo rje thal mo kha 'bus pa dang / dbus ma dang / mthe bong dang / mthe chung kha bye ba'i 'da' ma bzhin pa chos nyid thams

351b5(rgyud): gsungs shing bya rgyud du grags pas bzhin gzhag go zhes 'chad do// 'on kyang rnal 'byor gyi dbang mga' zhig gis gsungs nas/ bya rgyud ni ma yin
351b6(rgyud): te/ bdag gi rnal 'byor mang du bstan pa dang / spyod pa ci bde bas 'grub pa mang du bstan pa'i phyir ro// des na 'di rnal 'byor gyis rgyud yin te/
352a1(rgyud): ston pas rjes su gnang ba'i bka' dang / 'jam dpal
352a2(rgyud): gyis kyang / bya spyod rnal 'byor gyis rgyud thams cad las ma bsnyen yang 'grub pas na/
